   kośaḥ prājñair na dātavyo ye ca nāstikavṛttayaḥ // K_426 //	koSaH prAjQEH na dAtavyaH ye ca nAstika-vRttayaH // K_426 //
   mātāpitṛdvijaguru- bālastrīrājaghātinām /	mAtA-pitR-dvija-guru bAla-strI-rAja-GAtinAm /

   varṇasaṃkarajātānāṃ pāpābhyāsapravartinām // K_428 //	varNa-saMkara-jAtAnAm pApa-aByAsa-pravartinAm // K_428 //
   eteṣv evābhiyogeṣu nindyeṣv eva ca yatnataḥ /	etezu eva-aBiyogezu nindyezu eva ca yatnatas /

   mahāpātakayukteṣu nāstikeṣu viśeṣataḥ /	mahApAtaka-yuktezu nAstikezu viSezataH /
   na deyaṃ teṣu divyaṃ tu pāpābhyāsarateṣu ca // K_431 //	na deyam tezu divyam tu pApa-aByAsa-ratezu ca // K_431 //
   eṣu vādeṣu divyāni pratiṣiddhāni yatnataḥ /	ezu vAdezu divyAni pratizidDAni yatnatas /
   kārayet sajjanais tāni nābhiśastaṃ tyajen manuḥ // K_432 //	kArayet sat-janEH tAni na-aBiSastam tyajet manuH // K_432 //
   aspṛśyādhamadāsānāṃ mlecchānāṃ pāpakāriṇām /	aspRSya-aDama-dAsAnAm mlecCAnAm pApa-kAriNAm /
   prātilomyapasūtānāṃ niścayo na tu rājani /	prAtilomyapasUtAnAm niScayaH na tu rAjani /
   tatprasiddhāni divyāni saṃśaye teṣu nirdiśet // K_433 //	tad-prasidDAni divyAni saMSaye tezu nirdiSet // K_433 //
   [divyadeśāḥ]	[divya-deSAH]
   indrasthāne 'bhiśastānāṃ mahāpātakināṃ nṛṇām /	indra-sTAne aBiSastAnAm mahApAtakinAm nRNAm /
   nṛpadrohe pravṛttānāṃ rājadvāre prayojayet // K_434 //	nRpa-drohe pravRttAnAm rAjadvAre prayojayet // K_434 //
   prātilomyaprasūtānāṃ divyaṃ deyaṃ catuṣpathe /	prAtilomya-prasUtAnAm divyam deyam catuzpaTe /
   ato 'nyeṣu sabhāmadhye divyaṃ deyaṃ vidur budhāḥ // K_435 //	atas anyezu saBA-maDye divyam deyam viduH buDAH // K_435 //
   kāladeśavirodhe tu yathāyuktaṃ prakalpayet /	kAla-deSa-viroDe tu yaTA-yuktam prakalpayet /
   anyena hārayed divyaṃ vidhir eṣa viparyaye // K_436 //	anyena hArayet divyam viDiH eza viparyaye // K_436 //
   adeśakāladattāni bahirvāsakṛtāni ca /	adeSa-kAla-dattAni bahis-vAsa-kRtAni ca /
   vyabhicāraṃ sadārtheṣu kurvantīha na saṃśayaḥ // K_437 //	vyaBicAram sadA-arTezu kurvanti-iha na saMSayaH // K_437 //
   sādhayet tat punaḥ sādhyaṃ vyāghāte sādhanasya hi /	sADayet tat punar sADyam vyAGAte sADanasya hi /

   tasmād yathoktavidhinā divyaṃ deyaṃ viśāradaiḥ /	tasmAt yaTA-ukta-viDinA divyam deyam viSAradEH /

   śikyac chede tulābhaṅge tathā vāpi guṇasya vā /	Sikyat Cede tulA-BaFge taTA vA-api guNasya vA /
   śuddhes tu saṃśaye caiva parīkṣeta punar naram // K_440 //	SudDeH tu saMSaye ca-eva parIkzeta punar naram // K_440 //
   [agnidivyavidhiḥ]	[agni-divya-viDiH]
   praskhalaty abhiyuktaś cet sthānād anyatra dahyate /	prasKalati aBiyuktaH ced sTAnAt anyatra dahyate /
   na dagdhaṃ tu vidur devās tasya bhūyo 'pi dāpayet // K_441 //	na dagDam tu viduH devAH tasya BUyas api dApayet // K_441 //
   [udakadivyavidhiḥ]	[udaka-divya-viDiH]
   śarāṃs tv anāyasair agraiḥ prakurvīta viśuddhaye /	SarAn tu anAyasEH agrEH prakurvIta viSudDaye /
   veṇakāṇḍamayāṃś caiva kṣeptā ca sudṛḍhaṃ kṣipet // K_442 //	veNa-kANxa-mayAn ca-eva kzeptA ca su-dRXam kzipet // K_442 //
   kṣipte tu majjanaṃ kāryaṃ gamanaṃ samakālikam /	kzipte tu majjanam kAryam gamanam sama-kAlikam /
   gamane tv āgamaḥ kāryaḥ pumān anyo jale viśet // K_443 //	gamane tu AgamaH kAryaH pumAn anyaH jale viSet // K_443 //
   śiromānaṃ tu dṛśyeta na karṇau nāpi nāsikā /	SiraH-mAnam tu dRSyeta na karNO na-api nAsikA /

   nimajjyotplavate yas tu dṛṣṭaś cet prāṇibhir naraḥ /	nimajjya-utplavate yaH tu dRzwaH ced prANiBiH naraH /
   punas tatra nimajjet sa deśacihnavibhāvite // K_445 //	punar tatra nimajjet sa deSa-cihna-viBAvite // K_445 //
   [viṣadivyavidhiḥ]	[viza-divya-viDiH]
   ajāśṛṅganibhaṃ śyāmaṃ supīnaṃ śṛṅgasaṃbhavam /	ajA-SRFga-niBam SyAmam su-pInam SRFga-saMBavam /

   vatsanābhanibhaṃ pītaṃ varṇajñānena niścayaḥ /	vatsanABa-niBam pItam varNa-jQAnena niScayaH /

   bāhyam evaṃ samākhyātaṃ lakṣaṇaṃ dharmasādhakaiḥ // K_449 //	bAhyam evam samAKyAtam lakzaNam Darma-sADakEH // K_449 //
   pūrvāhṇe śītale deśe viṣaṃ dadyāt tu dehinām /	pUrvAhNe SItale deSe vizam dadyAt tu dehinAm /
   ghṛtena yojitaṃ ślakṣṇaṃ piṣṭaṃ triṃśadguṇena tu // K_450 //	GRtena yojitam SlakzNam pizwam triMSat-guNena tu // K_450 //
   viṣasya palaṣaḍbhāgād bhāgo viṃśatim astu yaḥ /	vizasya pala-zaz-BAgAt BAgaH viMSatim astu yaH /
   tam aṣṭabhāgahīnaṃ śodhye deyaṃ ghṛtāplutam // K_451 //	tam azwa-BAga-hInam SoDye deyam GRta-Aplutam // K_451 //
   [kośadivyavidhiḥ]	[koSa-divya-viDiH]
   svalpe 'parādhe devānāṃ snāpayitvāyudhodakam /	su-alpe aparADe devAnAm snApayitvA-AyuDa-udakam /
   pāyyo vikāre cāśuddho niyamyaḥ śucir anyathā // K_452 //	pAyyaH vikAre ca-aSudDaH niyamyaH SuciH anyaTA // K_452 //
   [taṇḍulavidhiḥ]	[taNxula-viDiH]
   devatāsnānapānīya- divye taṇḍulabhakṣaṇe /	devatA-snAna-pAnIya divye taNxula-BakzaNe /
   śuddhaniṣṭhīvanāc śuddho niyamyo 'śucir anyathā // K_453 //	SudDa-nizWIvanAt SudDaH niyamyaH aSuciH anyaTA // K_453 //
   avaṣṭambhābhiyuktasya viśuddhasyāpi kośataḥ /	avazwamBa-aBiyuktasya viSudDasya-api koSataH /
   sadaṇḍam abhiyogaṃ ca dāpayed abhiyojakam /	sa-daNxam aBiyogam ca dApayet aBiyojakam /
   divyena śuddhaṃ puruṣaṃ sat kuryād dhārmiko nṛpaḥ // K_454 //	divyena SudDam puruzam sat kuryAt DArmikaH nRpaH // K_454 //
   śoṇitaṃ dṛśyate yatra hanuvālaṃ ca sīdati /	SoNitam dRSyate yatra hanu-vAlam ca sIdati /
   gātraṃ ca kampate yasya tam aśuddhaṃ vinirdiśet // K_455 //	gAtram ca kampate yasya tam aSudDam vinirdiSet // K_455 //
   atha daivavisaṃvādāt trisaptāhāt tu dāpayet /	aTa dEva-visaMvAdAt tri-sapta-ahAt tu dApayet /
   abhiyuktaṃ tu yatnena tam arthaṃ daṇḍam eva ca // K_456 //	aBiyuktam tu yatnena tam arTam daNxam eva ca // K_456 //
   tasyaikasya na sarvasya janasya yadi tad bhavet /	tasya-ekasya na sarvasya janasya yadi tat Bavet /
   rogo 'gnir jñātimaraṇam ṛṇaṃ dāpyo damaṃ ca saḥ // K_457 //	rogaH agniH jQAti-maraNam RNam dApyaH damam ca saH // K_457 //
   kṣayātisāravisphoṭās tālvasthiparipīḍanam /	kzaya-atisAra-visPowAH tAlu-asTi-paripIxanam /
   netraruggalarogaś ca tathonmādaḥ prajāyate /	netra-ruj-gala-rogaH ca taTA-unmAdaH prajAyate /
   śirorugbhujabhaṅgaś ca daivikā vyādhayo nṛṇām // K_458 //	SiraH-ruj-Buja-BaFgaH ca dEvikAH vyADayaH nRNAm // K_458 //
   śatārdhaṃ dāpayec śuddham aśuddho daṇḍabhāg bhavet // K_459 //	Sata-arDam dApayet SudDam aSudDaH daNxa-BAj Bavet // K_459 //
   viṣe toye hutāśe ca tulākośe ca taṇḍule /	vize toye hutASe ca tulA-koSe ca taNxule /
   taptamāṣakadivye ca kramād daṇḍaṃ prakalpayet // K_460 //	tapta-mAzaka-divye ca kramAt daNxam prakalpayet // K_460 //
   sahasraṃ ṣaṭśataṃ caiva tathā pañca śatāni ca /	sahasram zaz-Satam ca-eva taTA paQca SatAni ca /
   catustridvyekam evaṃ ca hīnaṃ hīneṣu kalpayet // K_461 //	catur-tri-dvi-ekam evam ca hInam hInezu kalpayet // K_461 //
   [śapathavidhiḥ]	[SapaTa-viDiH]
   yatropadiśyate karma kartur aṅgaṃ na tūcyate /	yatra-upadiSyate karma kartuH aFgam na tu-ucyate /
   dakṣiṇas tatra vijñeyaḥ karmaṇāṃ pāragaḥ karaḥ // K_462 //	dakziNaH tatra vijQeyaH karmaNAm pAragaH karaH // K_462 //
   ācaturdaśakād ahno yasya no rājadaivikam /	AcaturdaSakAt ahnaH yasya naH rAja-dEvikam /
   vyasanaṃ jāyate ghoraṃ sa jñeyaḥ śapathe śuciḥ // K_463 //	vyasanam jAyate Goram sa jQeyaH SapaTe SuciH // K_463 //
   [unmattāsvatantrādikṛtānāṃ vicāraḥ]	[unmatta-asvatantra-Adi-kRtAnAm vicAraH]
   unmattenaiva mattena tathā bhāvāntareṇa vā /	unmattena-eva mattena taTA BAva-antareNa vA /
   yad dattaṃ yat kṛtaṃ vātha pramāṇaṃ naiva tad bhavet // K_464 //	yat dattam yat kRtam vA-aTa pramANam na-eva tat Bavet // K_464 //
   asvatantrakṛtaṃ kāryaṃ tasya svāmī nivartayet /	asvatantra-kRtam kAryam tasya svAmI nivartayet /
   na bhartrā vivadetānyo bhītonmattakṛtād ṛte // K_465 //	na BartrA vivadeta-anyaH BIta-unmatta-kRtAt Rte // K_465 //
   pitāsvatantraḥ pitṛmān bhrātā bhātṛvya eva vā /	pitA-asvatantraH pitRmAn BrAtA BAtRvyaH eva vA /
   kaniṣṭho vāvibhaktasvo dāsaḥ karmakaras tathā // K_466 //	kanizWaH vA-aviBakta-svaH dAsaH karmakaraH taTA // K_466 //
   na kṣetragṛhadāsānāṃ dānādhamanavikrayāḥ /	na kzetra-gRha-dAsAnAm dAna-ADamana-vikrayAH /
   asvatantrakṛtāḥ siddhiṃ prāpnuyur nānuvarṇitāḥ // K_467 //	asvatantra-kRtAH sidDim prApnuyuH na-anuvarNitAH // K_467 //
   pramāṇaṃ sarva evaite paṇyānāṃ krayavikraye /	pramANam sarve eva-ete paNyAnAm kraya-vikraye /
   yadi saṃvyavahāraṃ te kurvanto 'py anumoditāḥ // K_468 //	yadi saMvyavahAram te kurvantaH api anumoditAH // K_468 //
   kṣetrādīṇāṃ tathaiva syur bhrātā bhrātṛsutaḥ sutaḥ /	kzetra-AdINAm taTA-eva syuH BrAtA BrAtR-sutaH sutaH /
   nisṛṣṭāḥ kṛtyakaraṇe guruṇā yadi gacchatā // K_469 //	nisRzwAH kRtya-karaNe guruNA yadi gacCatA // K_469 //
   nisṛṣṭārthas tu yo yasmin tasminn arthe prabhus tu saḥ /	nisRzwa-arTaH tu yaH yasmin tasmin arTe praBuH tu saH /
   tadbhartā tatkṛtaṃ kāryaṃ nānyathā kartum arhati // K_470 //	tad-BartA tat-kRtam kAryam na-anyaTA kartum arhati // K_470 //
   sutasya sutadārāṇāṃ vaśitvaṃ tv anuśāsane /	sutasya suta-dArANAm vaSitvam tu anuSAsane /
   vikraye caiva dāne ca vaśitvaṃ na sute pituḥ // K_471 //	vikraye ca-eva dAne ca vaSitvam na sute pituH // K_471 //
   [nirṇayakṛtyam]	[nirNaya-kRtyam]
   śuddhis tu śāstratattvajñaiś cikitsā samudāhṛtā /	SudDiH tu SAstra-tattva-jQEH cikitsA samudAhRtA /
   prāyaścittaṃ ca daṇḍaṃ ca tābhyāṃ sā dvividhā smṛtā // K_472 //	prAyaScittam ca daNxam ca tAByAm sA dviviDA smRtA // K_472 //
   anekārthābhiyoge 'pi yāvat saṃsādhayed dhanī /	aneka-arTa-aBiyoge api yAvat saMsADayet DanI /
   sākṣibhis tāvad evāsau labhate sādhitaṃ dhanam // K_473 //	sAkziBiH tAvat eva-asO laBate sADitam Danam // K_473 //
   sarvāpalāpaṃ yaḥ kṛtvā mitho 'lpam api saṃvadet /	sarva-apalApam yaH kRtvA miTas alpam api saMvadet /
   sarvam eva tu dāpyaḥ syād abhiyukto bṛhaspatiḥ // K_474 //	sarvam eva tu dApyaH syAt aBiyuktaH bRhaspatiH // K_474 //
   evaṃ dharmāsanasthena samenaiva vivādinā /	evam Darma-Asana-sTena samena-eva vivAdinA /
   kāryāṇāṃ nirṇayo dṛśyo brāhmaṇaiḥ saha nānyathā // K_475 //	kAryANAm nirNayaH dRSyaH brAhmaNEH saha na-anyaTA // K_475 //
   vyavahārān svayaṃ dṛṣṭvā śrutvā vā prāṅvivākataḥ /	vyavahArAn svayam dRzwvA SrutvA vA prAFvivAkataH /
   jayapatraṃ tato dadyāt parijñānāya pārthivaḥ // K_476 //	jaya-patram tatas dadyAt parijQAnAya pArTivaH // K_476 //
   [daṇḍavidhiḥ]	[daNxa-viDiH]
   rājā tu svāmine vipraṃ sāntvenaiva pradāpayet /	rAjA tu svAmine vipram sAntvena-eva pradApayet /
   deśācāreṇa cānyāṃs tu duṣṭān saṃpīḍya dāpayet // K_477 //	deSa-AcAreNa ca-anyAn tu duzwAn saMpIxya dApayet // K_477 //
   rikthinaṃ suhṛdaṃ vāpi cchalenaiva pradāpayet /	rikTinam suhRdam vA-api cCalena-eva pradApayet /
   vaṇijaḥ karṣakāṃś cāpi śilpinaś cābravīd bhṛguḥ // K_478 //	vaNijaH karzakAn ca-api SilpinaH ca-abravIt BRguH // K_478 //
   dhanadānāsahaṃ buddhvā svādhīnaṃ karma kārayet /	Dana-dAna-asaham budDvA svADInam karma kArayet /
   aśaktau bandhanāgāraṃ praveśyo brāhmaṇād ṛte // K_479 //	aSaktO banDana-AgAram praveSyaH brAhmaNAt Rte // K_479 //
   karṣakān kṣatraviśśūdrān samīhānāṃs tu dāpayet // K_480 //	karzakAn kzatra-viS-SUdrAn samIhAnAn tu dApayet // K_480 //
   ācāryasya pitur mātur bāndhavānāṃ tathaiva ca /	AcAryasya pituH mAtuH bAnDavAnAm taTA-eva ca /
   eteṣām aparādheṣu daṇḍo naiva vidhīyate // K_481 //	etezAm aparADezu daNxaH na-eva viDIyate // K_481 //
   prāṇātyaye tu yatra syād akāryakaraṇaṃ kṛtam /	prANa-atyaye tu yatra syAt akArya-karaNam kRtam /
   daṇḍas tatra tu naiva syād eṣa dharmo bhṛgusmṛtaḥ // K_482 //	daNxaH tatra tu na-eva syAt eza DarmaH BRgu-smRtaH // K_482 //
   na jātu brāhmaṇaṃ hanyāt sarvapāpeṣv avasthitam /	na jAtu brAhmaNam hanyAt sarva-pApezu avasTitam /
   rāṣṭrāc cainaṃ bahiḥ kuryāt samagradhanam akṣatam // K_483 //	rAzwrAt ca-enam bahis kuryAt samagra-Danam akzatam // K_483 //
   caturṇām api varṇānāṃ prāyaścittam akurvatām /	caturNAm api varNAnAm prAyaScittam akurvatAm /
   śarīradhanasaṃyuktaṃ daṇḍaṃ dharmyaṃ prakalpayet // K_484 //	SarIra-Dana-saMyuktam daNxam Darmyam prakalpayet // K_484 //
   yena doṣeṇa śūdrasya daṇḍo bhavati dharmataḥ /	yena dozeNa SUdrasya daNxaH Bavati DarmataH /
   tena cet kṣatraviprāṇāṃ dviguṇo dviguṇo bhavet // K_485 //	tena ced kzatra-viprANAm dviguNaH dviguNaH Bavet // K_485 //
   pravrajyāvasitaṃ śūdraṃ japahomaparāyaṇam /	pravrajyA-vasitam SUdram japa-homa-parAyaNam /
   vadhena śāsayet pāpaṃ daṇḍyo vā dviguṇaṃ damam // K_486 //	vaDena SAsayet pApam daNxyaH vA dviguNam damam // K_486 //
   sarveṣu cāparādheṣu puṃso yo 'rthadamaḥ smṛtaḥ /	sarvezu ca-aparADezu puMsaH yaH arTa-damaH smRtaH /
   tadardhaṃ yoṣito dadyur vadhe puṃso 'ṅga kartanam // K_487 //	tad-arDam yozitaH dadyuH vaDe puMsaH aFga kartanam // K_487 //
   nāsvatantrāḥ striyo grāhyāḥ pumāṃs tatrāparādhyati /	na-asvatantrAH striyaH grAhyAH pumAn tatra-aparADyati /
   prabhuṇā śāsanīyās tā rājā tu puruṣaṃ nayet // K_488 //	praBuNA SAsanIyAH tAH rAjA tu puruzam nayet // K_488 //
   proṣitasvāmikā nārī prāpitā yady api grahe /	prozita-svAmikA nArI prApitA yadi api grahe /
   tāvat sā bandhane sthāpyā yāvat pratyāgataḥ prabhuḥ // K_489 //	tAvat sA banDane sTApyAH yAvat pratyAgataH praBuH // K_489 //
   kalpito yasya yo daṇḍas tv aparādhasya yatnataḥ /	kalpitaH yasya yaH daNxaH tu aparADasya yatnatas /
   paṇānāṃ grahaṇaṃ tu syāt tanmūlyaṃ vātha rājani // K_490 //	paNAnAm grahaNam tu syAt tad-mUlyam vA-aTa rAjani // K_490 //
   māṣapādo dvipādo vā daṇḍo yatra pravartitaḥ /	mAzapAdaH dvi-pAdaH vA daNxaH yatra pravartitaH /
   anirdiṣṭaṃ tu vijñeyaṃ māṣakaṃ tu prakalpayet // K_491 //	anirdizwam tu vijQeyam mAzakam tu prakalpayet // K_491 //
   yatrokto māṣakair daṇḍo rājataṃ tatra nirdiśeta /	yatra-uktaH mAzakEH daNxaH rAjatam tatra nirdiSeta /
   kṛṣṇalaiś coktam eva syād uktadaṇḍaviniścayaḥ // K_492 //	kRzNalEH ca-uktam eva syAt ukta-daNxa-viniScayaH // K_492 //
   māṣo viṃśatibhāgas tu jñeyaḥ kārṣāpaṇasya tu /	mAzaH viMSati-BAgaH tu jQeyaH kArzApaNasya tu /
   kākaṇī tu caturbhāgā māṣakasya paṇasya ca // K_493 //	kAkaNI tu catur-BAgAH mAzakasya paNasya ca // K_493 //
   pañcanadyāḥ pradeśe tu saṃjñeyaṃ vyavahārikī /	paQcanadyAH pradeSe tu saMjQA-iyam vyavahArikI /
   kārṣāpaṇoṇḍikā jñeyās tāś catasras tu dhānakaḥ /	kArzApaNa-uNxikAH jQeyAH tAH catasraH tu DAnakaH /
   te dvādaśa suvarṇās tu dīnāraś citrakaḥ smṛtaḥ // K_494 //	te dvAdaSa suvarNAH tu dInAraH citrakaH smRtaH // K_494 //
   [punarnyāyaḥ]	[punar-nyAyaH]
   asat sad iti yaḥ pakṣaḥ sabhyair evāvadhāryate /	asat sat iti yaH pakzaH saByEH eva-avaDAryate /
   tīritaḥ so 'nuśiṣṭas tu sākṣivākyāt prakīrtitaḥ // K_495 //	tIritaH saH anuSizwaH tu sAkzi-vAkyAt prakIrtitaH // K_495 //
   kulādibhir niścite 'pi santoṣaṃ na gatas tu yaḥ /	kula-AdiBiH niScite api santozam na gataH tu yaH /
   vicārya tat kṛtaṃ rājā kukṛtaṃ punar uddharet // K_496 //	vicArya tat kRtam rAjA kukRtam punar udDaret // K_496 //
   [ṛṇādāne vṛddhivicāraḥ]	[RNa-AdAne vRdDi-vicAraH]
   na strībhyo dāsabālebhyaḥ prayacchet kvacid uddhṛtam /	na strIByaH dAsa-bAleByaH prayacCet kvacid udDRtam /
   dātā na labhate tat tu tebhyo dadyāt tu yad vasu // K_497 //	dAtA na laBate tat tu teByaH dadyAt tu yat vasu // K_497 //
   ṛṇikena tu yā vṛddhir adhikā saṃprakalpitā /	RNikena tu yA vRdDiH aDikA saMprakalpitA /
   āpatkālakṛtā nityaṃ dātavyā kāritā tu sā /	Apad-kAla-kRtA nityam dAtavyA kAritA tu sA /
   anyathā kāritā vṛddhir na dātavyā kathaṃcana // K_498 //	anyaTA kAritA vRdDiH na dAtavyA kaTaMcana // K_498 //
   ekāntenaiva vṛddhiṃ tu śodhayed yatra carṇikam /	ekAntena-eva vRdDim tu SoDayet yatra ca-RNikam /
   pratikālaṃ dadāty eva śikhāvṛddhis tu sā smṛtā // K_499 //	pratikAlam dadAti eva SiKA-vRdDiH tu sA smRtA // K_499 //
   gṛhāt toṣaḥ phalaṃ kṣetrād bhogalābhaḥ prakīrtitaḥ // K_500 //	gRhAt tozaH Palam kzetrAt Boga-lABaH prakIrtitaH // K_500 //
   ādhibhogas tv aśeṣo yo vṛddhis tu parikalpitaḥ /	ADi-BogaH tu aSezaH yaH vRdDiH tu parikalpitaH /
   prayogo yatra caivaṃ syād ādhibhogaḥ sa ucyate // K_501 //	prayogaH yatra ca-evam syAt ADiBogaH saH ucyate // K_501 //
   [ākṛtavṛddhiḥ]	[a-akRtavRdDiH]
   yo yācitakam ādāya tam adattvā diśaṃ vrajet /	yaH yAcitakam AdAya tam adattvA diSam vrajet /
   ūrdhvaṃ saṃvatsarāt tasya taddhanaṃ vṛddhim āpnuyāt // K_502 //	UrDvam saMvatsarAt tasya tat-Danam vRdDim ApnuyAt // K_502 //
   kṛtvoddhāram adattvā yo yācitas tu diśaṃ vrajet /	kRtvA-udDAram adattvA yaH yAcitaH tu diSam vrajet /
   ūrdhvaṃ māsatrayāt tasya taddhanaṃ vṛddhim āpnuyāt // K_503 //	UrDvam mAsa-trayAt tasya tat-Danam vRdDim ApnuyAt // K_503 //
   svadeśe 'pi sthito yas tu na dadyād yācitaḥ kvacit /	sva-deSe api sTitaH yaH tu na dadyAt yAcitaH kvacid /
   taṃ tato 'kāritāṃ vṛddhim anicchantaṃ ca dāpayet // K_504 //	tam tatas akAritAm vRdDim anicCantam ca dApayet // K_504 //
   prītidattaṃ na vardheta yāvan na pratiyācitam /	prIti-dattam na varDeta yAvat na pratiyAcitam /
   yācyamānam adattaṃ ced vardhate pañcakaṃ śatam // K_505 //	yAcyamAnam adattam ced varDate paQcakam Satam // K_505 //
   nikṣiptaṃ vṛddhiśeṣaṃ ca krayavikrayam eva ca /	nikziptam vRdDi-Sezam ca kraya-vikrayam eva ca /
   yācyamānam adattaṃ ced vardhate pañcakaṃ śatam // K_506 //	yAcyamAnam adattam ced varDate paQcakam Satam // K_506 //
   paṇyaṃ gṛhītvā yo mūlyam adattvaiva diśaṃ vrajet /	paNyam gRhItvA yaH mUlyam adattvA-eva diSam vrajet /
   ṛtutrayasyāpariṣṭāt taddhanaṃ vṛddhim āpnuyāt // K_507 //	Rtu-trayasya-aparizwAt tat-Danam vRdDim ApnuyAt // K_507 //
   carmasasyāsavadyūte paṇyamūlye ca sarvadā /	carma-sasya-Asava-dyUte paNya-mUlye ca sarvadA /
   strīśulkeṣu na vṛddhiḥ syāt prātibhāvyāgateṣu ca // K_508 //	strI-Sulkezu na vRdDiH syAt prAtiBAvya-Agatezu ca // K_508 //
   [vṛddheḥ parimāṇaṃ]	[vRdDeH parimANaM]
   grāhyaṃ syād dviguṇaṃ dravyaṃ prayuktaṃ dhanināṃ sadā /	grAhyam syAt dviguNam dravyam prayuktam DaninAm sadA /
   labhate cen na dviguṇaṃ punar vṛddhiṃ prakalpayet // K_509 //	laBate ced na dviguNam punar vRdDim prakalpayet // K_509 //
   maṇimuktāpravālānāṃ suvarṇarajatasya ca /	maNi-muktA-pravAlAnAm suvarNa-rajatasya ca /
   tiṣṭhati dviguṇā vṛddhiḥ phālakaiṭāvikasya ca // K_510 //	tizWati dviguNA vRdDiH PAla-kEwa-Avikasya ca // K_510 //
   tailānāṃ caiva sarveṣāṃ madyānām atha sarpiṣām /	tElAnAm ca-eva sarvezAm madyAnAm aTa sarpizAm /
   vṛddhir aṣṭaguṇā jñeyā guḍasya lavaṇasya ca // K_511 //	vRdDiH azwaguNAH jQeyAH guxasya lavaNasya ca // K_511 //
   kupyaṃ pañcaguṇaṃ bhūmis tathaivāṣṭaguṇā matā /	kupyam paQcaguNam BUmiH taTA-eva-azwaguNA matA /
   sadya eveti vacanāt sadya eva pradīyate // K_512 //	sadyas eva-iti vacanAt sadyas eva pradIyate // K_512 //
   [ṛṇoddharaṇaṃ]	[RNot-haraNaM]
   [anekarṇasamavāye vidhiḥ]	[anekarNa-samavAye viDiH]
   ekāhe likhitaṃ yat tu tat tu kuryād ṛṇaṃ samam /	eka-ahe liKitam yat tu tat tu kuryAt RNam samam /
   grahaṇaṃ rakṣaṇaṃ lābham anyathā tu yathākramam // K_513 //	grahaNam rakzaNam lABam anyaTA tu yaTAkramam // K_513 //
   nānāṛṇasamavāye tu yad yat pūrvakṛtaṃ bhavet /	nAnA-aRNa-samavAye tu yat yat pUrva-kRtam Bavet /
   tat tad evāgrato deyaṃ rājñaḥ syāc śrotriyād anu // K_514 //	tat tat eva-agratas deyam rAjQaH syAt SrotriyAt anu // K_514 //
   yasya dravyeṇa yat paṇyaṃ sādhitaṃ yo vibhāvayet /	yasya dravyeNa yat paNyam sADitam yaH viBAvayet /
   tad dravyam ṛṇikenaiva dātavyaṃ tasya nānyathā // K_515 //	tat dravyam RNikena-eva dAtavyam tasya na-anyaTA // K_515 //
   [ādhiḥ]	[ADiH]
   dravyaṃ gṛhītvā vṛddhyarthaṃ bhogayogyaṃ dadāti cet /	dravyam gRhItvA vRdDi-arTam Boga-yogyam dadAti ced /
   jaṅgamaṃ sthāvaraṃ vāpi bhogyādhiḥ sa tu kathyate /	jaFgamam sTAvaram vA-api Bogya-ADiH sa tu kaTyate /
   mūlyaṃ tadādhikaṃ dattvā svakṣetrādikam āpnuyāt // K_516 //	mUlyam tadA-aDikam dattvA sva-kzetra-Adikam ApnuyAt // K_516 //
   ādhim ekaṃ dvayor yas tu kuryāt kā pratipad bhavet /	ADim ekam dvayoH yaH tu kuryAt kA pratipad Bavet /
   tayoḥ pūrvakṛtaṃ grāhyaṃ tatkartā coradaṇḍabhāk // K_517 //	tayoH pUrva-kRtam grAhyam tad-kartA cora-daNxa-BAj // K_517 //
   ādhānaṃ vikrayo dānaṃ lekhyasākṣyakṛtaṃ yadā /	ADAnam vikrayaH dAnam leKya-sAkzya-kRtam yadA /
   ekakriyāviruddhaṃ tu lekhyaṃ tatrāpahārakam // K_518 //	eka-kriyA-virudDam tu leKyam tatra-apahArakam // K_518 //
   anirdiṣṭaṃ ca nirdiṣṭam ekatra ca vilekhitam /	anirdizwam ca nirdizwam ekatra ca vileKitam /

   yo 'vidyamānaṃ prathamam anirdiṣṭasvarūpakam /	yaH avidyamAnam praTamam anirdizwa-svarUpakam /
   ākāśabhūtam ādadhyād anirdiṣṭaṃ ca tad bhavet /	AkASa-BUtam AdaDyAt anirdizwam ca tat Bavet /
   yad yat tadāsya vidyeta tad ādiṣṭaṃ vinirdiśet // K_520 //	yat yat tadA-asya vidyeta tat Adizwam vinirdiSet // K_520 //
   yas tu sarvasvam ādiśya prāk paścān nāmacihnitam /	yaH tu sarva-svam AdiSya prAk paScAt nAma-cihnitam /
   ādadhyāt tat kathaṃ na syāc cihnitaṃ balavattaram // K_521 //	AdaDyAt tat kaTam na syAt cihnitam balavattaram // K_521 //
   maryādācihnitaṃ kṣetraṃ grāmaṃ vāpi yadā bhavet /	maryAdA-cihnitam kzetram grAmam vA-api yadA Bavet /
   grāmādayaś ca likhyante tadā siddhim avāpnuyāt // K_522 //	grAma-AdayaH ca liKyante tadA sidDim avApnuyAt // K_522 //
   ādhīkṛtaṃ tu yat kiṃcid vinaṣṭaṃ daivarājataḥ /	ADIkRtam tu yat kiMcid vinazwam dEva-rAjataH /
   tatra ṛṇaṃ sodayaṃ dāpyo dhaninām adhamarṇakaḥ // K_523 //	tatra RNam sa-udayam dApyaH DaninAm aDamarNakaH // K_523 //
   na ced dhanikadoṣeṇa nipated vā mriyeta vā /	na ced Danika-dozeNa nipatet vA mriyeta vA /
   ādhim anyaṃ sa dāpyaḥ syād ṛṇān mucyeta narṇikaḥ // K_524 //	ADim anyam sa dApyaH syAt RNAt mucyeta na-RNikaH // K_524 //
   akāmam ananujñātam adhiṃ yaḥ karma kārayet /	akAmam ananujQAtam aDim yaH karma kArayet /
   bhoktā karmaphalaṃ dāpyo vṛddhiṃ vā labhate na saḥ // K_525 //	BoktA karma-Palam dApyaH vRdDim vA laBate na saH // K_525 //
   yas tv ādhiṃ karma kurvāṇaṃ vācā daṇḍena karmabhiḥ /	yaH tu ADim karma kurvANam vAcA daNxena karmaBiH /
   pīḍayed bhatsayec caiva prāpnuyāt pūrvasāhasam // K_526 //	pIxayet Batsayet ca-eva prApnuyAt pUrva-sAhasam // K_526 //
   balādakāmaṃ yatrādhim anisṛṣṭaṃ praveśayet /	balAt-akAmam yatra-ADim anisRzwam praveSayet /
   prāpnuyāt sāhasaṃ pūrvam ādhātā cādhim āpnuyāt // K_527 //	prApnuyAt sAhasam pUrvam ADAtA ca-ADim ApnuyAt // K_527 //
   ādhiṃ duṣṭena lekhyena bhuṅkte yam ṛṇikād dhanī /	ADim duzwena leKyena BuFkte yam RNikAt DanI /

   ādhātā yatra na syāt tu dhanī bandhaṃ nivedayet /	ADAtA yatra na syAt tu DanI banDam nivedayet /
   rājñas tataḥ sa vikhyāto vikreya iti dhāraṇā /	rAjQaH tatas sa viKyAtaH vikreyaH iti DAraNA /
   savṛddhikaṃ gṛhītvā tu śeṣaṃ rājan yathārpayet // K_529 //	sa-vRdDikam gRhItvA tu Sezam rAjan yaTA-arpayet // K_529 //
   [pratibhūvidhānam]	[pratiBU-viDAnam]
   dānopasthānavādeṣu viśvāsaśapathāya ca /	dAna-upasTAna-vAdezu viSvAsa-SapaTAya ca /
   lagnakaṃ kārayed evaṃ yathāyogaṃ viparyaye // K_530 //	lagnakam kArayet evam yaTAyogam viparyaye // K_530 //
   darśanapratibhūryas taṃ deśe kāle na darśayet /	darSana-pratiBUH-yaH tam deSe kAle na darSayet /
   nibandham āvahet tatra daivarājakṛtād ṛte // K_531 //	nibanDam Avahet tatra dEva-rAja-kRtAt Rte // K_531 //
   naṣṭasyānveṣaṇārthaṃ tu deyaṃ pakṣatrayaṃ param /	nazwasya-anvezaNa-arTam tu deyam pakza-trayam param /
   yady asau darśayet tatra moktavyaḥ pratibhūr bhavet // K_532 //	yadi asO darSayet tatra moktavyaH pratiBUH Bavet // K_532 //
   kāle vyatīte pratibhūr yadi taṃ naiva darśayet /	kAle vyatIte pratiBUH yadi tam na-eva darSayet /
   sa tam arthaṃ pradāpyaḥ syāt prete caivaṃ vidhīyate // K_533 //	sa tam arTam pradApyaH syAt prete ca-evam viDIyate // K_533 //
   gṛhītvā bandhakaṃ yatra darśane 'sya sthito bhavet /	gRhItvA banDakam yatra darSane asya sTitaH Bavet /
   vinā pitrā dhanaṃ tasmād dāpyaḥ syāt tad ṛṇaṃ sutaḥ // K_534 //	vinA pitrA Danam tasmAt dApyaH syAt tat RNam sutaH // K_534 //
   yo yasya pratibhūs tiṣṭhed darśanāyeha mānavaḥ /	yaH yasya pratiBUH tizWet darSanAya-iha mAnavaH /
   adarśayan sa taṃ tasmai prayacchet svadhanād ṛṇam // K_535 //	adarSayan sa tam tasmE prayacCet sva-DanAt RNam // K_535 //
   ādyau tu vitathe dāpyau tatkālāveditaṃ dhanam /	AdyO tu vitaTe dApyO tad-kAla-Aveditam Danam /
   uttarau tu visaṃvāde tau vinā tatsutau tathā // K_536 //	uttarO tu visaMvAde tO vinA tad-sutO taTA // K_536 //
   ekacchāyāśrite sarvaṃ dadyāt tu proṣite sutaḥ /	ekacCAyA-ASrite sarvam dadyAt tu prozite sutaH /
   mṛte pitari pitṛaṃśaṃ pararṇaṃ na bṛhaspatiḥ // K_537 //	mRte pitari pitR-aMSam para-RNam na bRhaspatiH // K_537 //
   ekacchāyāpraviṣṭānāṃ dāpyo tas tatra dṛśyate /	eka=-CAyA-pravizwAnAm dApyaH tas tatra dRSyate /
   proṣite tatsutaḥ sarvaṃ pitraṃśaṃ tu mṛte sutaḥ // K_538 //	prozite tad-sutaH sarvam pitR-aMSam tu mRte sutaH // K_538 //
   prātibhāvyaṃ tu yo dadyāt pīḍitaḥ pratibhāvitaḥ /	prAtiBAvyam tu yaH dadyAt pIxitaH pratiBAvitaH /
   tripakṣāt parataḥ so 'rthaṃ dviguṇaṃ labdhum arhati // K_539 //	tri-pakzAt paratas saH arTam dviguNam labDum arhati // K_539 //
   yasyārthe yena yad dattaṃ vidhinābhyarthitena tu /	yasya-arTe yena yat dattam viDinA-aByarTitena tu /
   sākṣibhir bhāvitenaiva pratibhūs tat samāpnuyāt // K_540 //	sAkziBiH BAvitena-eva pratiBUH tat samApnuyAt // K_540 //
   satyaṃkāravisaṃvāde dviguṇaṃ pratidāpayet /	satyaMkAra-visaMvAde dviguNam pratidApayet /
   akurvatas tu tad dhāni satyaṃkāraprayojanam // K_541 //	akurvataH tu tat DAni satyaMkAra-prayojanam // K_541 //
   [pitrādibhiḥ kṛtam ṛṇaṃ kena pratideyam]	[pitR-AdiBiH kRtam RNam kena pratideyam]
   kuṭumbārtham aśaktena gṛhītaṃ vyādhitena vā /	kuwumba-arTam aSaktena gRhItam vyADitena vA /
   upaplavanimitte ca vidyād āpatkṛte tu tat // K_542 //	upaplava-nimitte ca vidyAt Apad-kRte tu tat // K_542 //
   kanyāvaivāhikaṃ caiva pretakārye ca yatkṛtam /	kanyA-vEvAhikam ca-eva pretakArye ca yat-kRtam /
   etat sarvaṃ pradātavyaṃ kuṭumbena kṛtaṃ prabhoḥ // K_543 //	etat sarvam pradAtavyam kuwumbena kRtam praBoH // K_543 //
   ṛṇaṃ putrakṛtaṃ pitrā na deyam iti dharmataḥ /	RNam putra-kRtam pitrA na deyam iti DarmataH /
   deyaṃ pratiśrutaṃ yat syāt yac ca syād anumoditam // K_544 //	deyam pratiSrutam yat syAt yat ca syAt anumoditam // K_544 //
   proṣitasyāmatenāpi kuṭumbārtham ṛṇaṃ kṛtam /	prozitasya-Amatena-api kuwumba-arTam RNam kRtam /
   dāsastrīmātṛśiṣyair vā dadyāt putreṇa vā bhṛguḥ // K_545 //	dAsa-strI-mAtR-SizyEH vA dadyAt putreNa vA BRguH // K_545 //
   bhartrā putreṇa vā sārdhaṃ kevalenātmanā kṛtam /	BartrA putreNa vA sArDam kevalena-AtmanA kRtam /
   ṛṇam evaṃvidhaṃ deyaṃ nānyathā tatkṛtaṃ striyā // K_546 //	RNam evaMviDam deyam na-anyaTA tat-kRtam striyAH // K_546 //
   martukāmena yā bhartrā proktā deyam ṛṇaṃ tvayā /	martu-kAmena yA BartrA proktA deyam RNam tvayA /
   aprapannāpi sā dāpyā dhanaṃ yady āśritaṃ striyām // K_547 //	aprapannA-api sA dApyAH Danam yadi ASritam striyAm // K_547 //
   vidyamāneapi rogārte svadeśāt proṣite 'pi vā /	vidyamAnA-iapi roga-Arte sva-deSAt prozite api vA /
   viṃśāt saṃvatsarād deyaṃ ṛṇaṃ pitṛkṛtaṃ sutaiḥ // K_548 //	viMSAt saMvatsarAt deyam RNam pitR-kRtam sutEH // K_548 //
   vyādhitonmattavṛddhānāṃ tathā dīrghapravāsinām /	vyADita-unmatta-vRdDAnAm taTA dIrGa-pravAsinAm /

   jātyandhapatitonmatta- kṣayaśvitrādirogiṇaḥ // K_550 //	jAti-anDa-patita-unmatta kzaya-Svitra-Adi-rogiNaH // K_550 //
   pitṝṇāṃ sūnubhir jātair dānenaivādhamād ṛṇāt /	pitLNAm sUnuBiH jAtEH dAnena-eva-aDamAt RNAt /
   vimokṣas tu yatas tasmād icchanti pitaraḥ sutān // K_551 //	vimokzaH tu yatas tasmAt icCanti pitaraH sutAn // K_551 //
   nāprāptavyavahāreṇa pitary uparate kvacit /	na-aprApta-vyavahAreNa pitari uparate kvacid /

   svātantryaṃ hi smṛtaṃ jyeṣṭhe jyaiṣṭhe guṇavayaḥkṛtam // K_553 //	svAtantryam hi smRtam jyezWe jyEzWe guNa-vayaH-kRtam // K_553 //
   yad dṛṣṭaṃ dattaśeṣaṃ vā deyaṃ paitāmahaṃ tu tat /	yat dRzwam datta-Sezam vA deyam pEtAmaham tu tat /
   sadoṣaṃ vyāhataṃ pitrā naiva deyam ṛṇaṃ kvacit // K_554 //	sa-dozam vyAhatam pitrA na-eva deyam RNam kvacid // K_554 //
   pitrā dṛṣṭam ṛṇaṃ yat tu kramāyātaṃ pitāmahāt /	pitrA dRzwam RNam yat tu krama-AyAtam pitAmahAt /
   nirdoṣaṃ noddhṛtaṃ putrair deyaṃ pautrais tu tadbhṛguḥ // K_555 //	nirdozam na-udDRtam putrEH deyam pOtrEH tu tad-BRguH // K_555 //
   paitāmahaṃ tu yat putrair na dattaṃ rogibhiḥ sthitaiḥ /	pEtAmaham tu yat putrEH na dattam rogiBiH sTitEH /
   tasmād evaṃvidhaṃ pautrair deyaṃ paitāmahaṃ samam // K_556 //	tasmAt evaMviDam pOtrEH deyam pEtAmaham samam // K_556 //
   ṛṇaṃ tu dāpayet putraṃ yadi syān nirupadravaḥ /	RNam tu dApayet putram yadi syAt nirupadravaH /

   yad deyaṃ pitṛbhir nityaṃ tadabhāve tu taddhanāt /	yat deyam pitRBiH nityam tad-aBAve tu tad-DanAt /

   pitrarṇe vidyamāne tu na ca putro dhanaṃ haret /	pitrA-RNe vidyamAne tu na ca putraH Danam haret /

   putrābhāve tu dātavyam ṛṇaṃ pautreṇa yatnataḥ /	putra-aBAve tu dAtavyam RNam pOtreNa yatnatas /
   caturthena na dātavyaṃ tasmāt tad vinirvartate // K_560 //	caturTena na dAtavyam tasmAt tat vinirvartate // K_560 //
   prātibhāvyāgataṃ pautrair dātavyaṃ na tu tatkvacit /	prAtiBAvya-Agatam pOtrEH dAtavyam na tu tad-kvacid /

   rikthahartrā ṛṇaṃ deyaṃ tadabhāve ca yoṣitaḥ /	rikTa-hartrA RNam deyam tad-aBAve ca yozitaH /
   putraiś ca tadabhāve 'nyai rikthabhāgbhir yathākramam // K_562 //	putrEH ca tad-aBAve anyEH rikTa-BAgBiH yaTAkramam // K_562 //

   likhitaṃ muktakaṃ vāpi deyaṃ yat tu pratiśrutam /	liKitam muktakam vA-api deyam yat tu pratiSrutam /
   parapūrvastriyai yat tu vidyāt kāmakṛtaṃ nṛṇām // K_564 //	parapUrva-striyE yat tu vidyAt kAma-kRtam nRNAm // K_564 //

   uktaṃ tuṣṭikaraṃ yat tu vidyād krodhakṛtaṃ tu tat // K_565 //	uktam tuzwi-karam yat tu vidyAt kroDa-kRtam tu tat // K_565 //
   svasthenārtena vā deyaṃ bhāvitaṃ dharmakāraṇāt /	svasTena-Artena vA deyam BAvitam Darma-kAraNAt /

   āpatkṛtād ṛte puṃsāṃ kuṭumbārthe hi vistaraḥ // K_569 //	Apad-kRtAt Rte puMsAm kuwumba-arTe hi vistaraH // K_569 //
   anyatra rajakavyādha- gopaśauṇḍikayoṣitām /	anyatra rajaka-vyADa gopa-SONxika-yozitAm /

   ṛṇārtham āharet tantuṃ na sukhārthaṃ kadācana /	RNa-arTam Aharet tantum na suKa-arTam kadAcana /

   yā svaputraṃ tu jahyāt strī samartham api putriṇī /	yA sva-putram tu jahyAt strI samarTam api putriNI /

   bālaputrādhikārthā ca bhartāraṃ yānyam āśritā /	bAla-putra-aDika-arTA ca BartAram yA-anyam ASritA /
   āśritas tadṛṇaṃ dadyād bālaputrāvidhiḥ smṛtaḥ // K_574 //	ASritaH tat-RNam dadyAt bAla-putrA-viDiH smRtaH // K_574 //
   dīrghapravāsinirbandhu- jaḍonmattārtaliṅginām /	dIrGa-pravAsi-nirbanDu jaxa-unmatta-Arta-liFginAm /

   vyasanābhiplute putre bālo vā yatna dṛśyate /	vyasana-aBiplute putre bAlaH vA yatna dRSyate /
   dravyahṛd dāpyate tatra tasyābhāve purandhrihṛt // K_576 //	dravya-hRt dApyate tatra tasya-aBAve puranDri-hRt // K_576 //
   pūrvaṃ dadyād dhanagrāhaḥ putras tasmād anantaram /	pUrvam dadyAt Dana-grAhaH putraH tasmAt anantaram /
   yoṣidgrāhaḥ sutābhāve putro vātyantanirdhanaḥ // K_577 //	yozit-grAhaH suta-aBAve putraH vA-atyanta-nirDanaH // K_577 //
   deyaṃ bhāryākṛtam ṛṇaṃ bhartrā putreṇa mātṛkam /	deyam BAryA-akRtam RNam BartrA putreNa mAtRkam /
   bhartur arthe kṛtaṃ yat syād abhidhāya gate diśam // K_578 //	BartuH arTe kRtam yat syAt aBiDAya gate diSam // K_578 //
   deyaṃ putrakṛtaṃ tat syād yac ca syād anuvarṇitam /	deyam putra-kRtam tat syAt yat ca syAt anuvarNitam /
   kṛtāsaṃvāditaṃ yac ca śrutvā caivānucoditam // K_579 //	kRtA-saMvAditam yat ca SrutvA ca-eva-anucoditam // K_579 //
   [adharmaṇikasyāvarodhādinā dhanoddhāravicāra]	[aDarmaNikasya-avaroDa-AdinA Dana-udDAra-vicAra]
   dhāryo 'varuddhas tv ṛṇikaḥ prakāśaṃ janasaṃsadi /	DAryaH avarudDaH tu RNikaH prakASam jana-saMsadi /
   yāvan na dadyād deyaṃ ca deśācārasthitir yathā // K_580 //	yAvat na dadyAt deyam ca deSa-AcAra-sTitiH yaTA // K_580 //
   viṇmūtraśaṅkā yasya syād dhāryamāṇasya dehinaḥ /	viz-mUtra-SaFkA yasya syAt DAryamANasya dehinaH /
   pṛṣṭhato vānugantavyo nibaddhaṃ vā samutsṛjet // K_581 //	pRzWatas vA-anugantavyaH nibadDam vA samutsRjet // K_581 //
   sa kṛtapratibhūś caiva moktavyaḥ syād dine dine /	sa kRta-pratiBUH ca-eva moktavyaH syAt dine dine /
   āhārakāle rātrau ca nibandhe pratibhūḥ sthitaḥ // K_582 //	AhAra-kAle rAtrO ca nibanDe pratiBUH sTitaH // K_582 //
   yo darśanapratibhuvaṃ nādhigacchen na cāśrayet /	yaH darSana-pratiBuvam na-aDigacCet na ca-ASrayet /
   sa cārake niroddhavyaḥ sthāpyo vāvedya rakṣiṇaḥ // K_583 //	sa cArake nirodDavyaH sTApyaH vA-Avedya rakziNaH // K_583 //
   na cārake niroddhavya āryaḥ prātyayikaḥ śuciḥ /	na cArake nirodDavyaH AryaH prAtyayikaH SuciH /
   so 'nibaddhaḥ pramoktavyo nibaddhaḥ śapathena vā // K_584 //	saH anibadDaH pramoktavyaH nibadDaH SapaTena vA // K_584 //
   pīḍanenoparodhena sādhayed ṛṇikaṃ dhanī /	pIxanena-uparoDena sADayet RNikam DanI /
   karmaṇā vyavahāreṇa sāntvenādau vibhāvitaḥ // K_585 //	karmaNA vyavahAreNa sAntvena-AdO viBAvitaH // K_585 //
   ādadītārtham evaṃ tu vyājenācaritena ca /	AdadIta-arTam evam tu vyAjena-Acaritena ca /
   karmaṇā kṣatraviśśūdrān samahīnāṃś ca dāpayet // K_586 //	karmaNA kzatra-viS-SUdrAn sama-hInAn ca dApayet // K_586 //
   rājānaṃ svāminaṃ vipraṃ sāntvenaiva pradāpayet /	rAjAnam svAminam vipram sAntvena-eva pradApayet /
   rikthinaṃ suhṛdaṃ vāpi cchalenaiva prasādhayet // K_587 //	rikTinam suhRdam vA-api cCalena-eva prasADayet // K_587 //
   vaṇijaḥ karṣakāś caiva śilpinaś cābravīd bhṛguḥ /	vaNijaH karzakAH ca-eva SilpinaH ca-abravIt BRguH /
   deśācāreṇa dāpyāḥ syur duṣṭān saṃpīḍya dāpayet // K_588 //	deSa-AcAreNa dApyAH syuH duzwAn saMpIxya dApayet // K_588 //
   pīḍayet tu dhanī yatra ṛṇikaṃ nyāyavādinam /	pIxayet tu DanI yatra RNikam nyAya-vAdinam /
   tasmād arthāt sa hīyeta tatsamaṃ cāpnuyād damam // K_589 //	tasmAt arTAt sa hIyeta tad-samam ca-ApnuyAt damam // K_589 //
   yadi hy ādāv anādiṣṭam aśubhaṃ karma kārayet /	yadi hi AdO anAdizwam aSuBam karma kArayet /
   prāpnuyāt sāhasaṃ pūrvam ṛṇān mucyeta carṇikaḥ // K_590 //	prApnuyAt sAhasam pUrvam RNAt mucyeta ca-RNikaH // K_590 //
   uddhārādikam ādāya svāmine na dadāti yaḥ /	udDAra-Adikam AdAya svAmine na dadAti yaH /
   sa tasya dāso bhṛtyaḥ strī paśur vā jāyate gṛhe // K_591 //	sa tasya dAsaH BRtyaH strI paSuH vA jAyate gRhe // K_591 //
   [upanidhiḥ]	[upaniDiH]
   trayaproṣitanikṣipta- bandhānvāhitayācitam /	traya-prozita-nikzipta banDa-anvAhita-yAcitam /
   vaiśyavṛttyarpitaṃ caiva so 'rthas tūpanidhiḥ smṛtaḥ // K_592 //	vESya-vRtti-arpitam ca-eva saH arTaH tu-upaniDiH smRtaH // K_592 //
   nikṣiptaṃ yasya yat kiṃcit tatprayatnena pālayet /	nikziptam yasya yat kiMcid tat-prayatnena pAlayet /
   daivarājakṛtād anyo vināśas tasya kīrtyate // K_593 //	dEva-rAja-kRtAt anyaH vinASaH tasya kIrtyate // K_593 //
   yasya doṣeṇa yat kiṃcid vināśyeta hriyeta vā /	yasya dozeNa yat kiMcid vinASyeta hriyeta vA /
   tad dravyaṃ sodayaṃ dāpyo daivarājakṛtād vinā // K_594 //	tat dravyam sa-udayam dApyaH dEva-rAja-kRtAt vinA // K_594 //
   yācitānantaraṃ nāśe daivarājakṛte 'pi saḥ /	yAcita-anantaram nASe dEva-rAja-kRte api saH /
   grahītā pratidāpyaḥ syān mūlyamātraṃ na saṃśayaḥ // K_595 //	grahItA pratidApyaH syAt mUlya-mAtram na saMSayaH // K_595 //
   nyāsādikaṃ paradravyaṃ prabhakṣitam upekṣitam /	nyAsa-Adikam para-dravyam praBakzitam upekzitam /
   ajñānanāśitaṃ caiva yena dāpyaḥ sa eva tat // K_596 //	ajQAna-nASitam ca-eva yena dApyaH saH eva tat // K_596 //
   bhakṣitaṃ sodayaṃ dāpyaḥ samaṃ dāpya upekṣitam /	Bakzitam sa-udayam dApyaH samam dApya upekzitam /
   kiṃcin nyūnaṃ pradāpyaḥ syād dravyam ajñānanāśitam // K_597 //	kiMcid nyUnam pradApyaH syAt dravyam ajQAna-nASitam // K_597 //
   arājadaivikenāpi nikṣiptaṃ yatra nāśitam /	arAja-dEvikena-api nikziptam yatra nASitam /
   grahītuḥ saha bhāṇḍena dātur naṣṭaṃ tad ucyate // K_598 //	grahItuH saha BANxena dAtuH nazwam tat ucyate // K_598 //
   jñātvā dravyaviyogaṃ tu dātā yatra vinikṣipet /	jQAtvA dravya-viyogam tu dAtA yatra vinikzipet /
   sarvopāyavināśe 'pi grahītā naiva dāpyate // K_599 //	sarva-upAya-vinASe api grahItA na-eva dApyate // K_599 //
   grāhakasya hi yad doṣān naṣṭaṃ tu grāhakasya tat /	grAhakasya hi yat dozAn nazwam tu grAhakasya tat /
   tasmin naṣṭe hṛte vāpi grahītā mūlyam āharet // K_600 //	tasmin nazwe hRte vA-api grahItA mUlyam Aharet // K_600 //
   grāhyas tūpanidhiḥ kāle kālahīnaṃ tu varjayet /	grAhyaH tu-upaniDiH kAle kAla-hInam tu varjayet /
   kālahīnaṃ dadaddaṇḍaṃ dviguṇaṃ ca pradāpyate // K_601 //	kAla-hInam dadat-daNxam dviguNam ca pradApyate // K_601 //
   sarveṣūpanidhiṣv ete vidhayaḥ parikīrtitāḥ // K_602 //	sarvezu-upaniDizu ete viDayaH parikIrtitAH // K_602 //
   yaiś ca saṃskriyate nyāso divasaiḥ pariniścitaiḥ /	yEH ca saMskriyate nyAsaH divasEH pariniScitEH /
   tadūrdhvaṃ sthāpayec śilpī dāpyo daivahate 'pi tat // K_603 //	tad-UrDvam sTApayet SilpI dApyaH dEva-hate api tat // K_603 //
   nyāsadoṣād vināśaḥ syāc śilpinaṃ tan na dāpayet /	nyAsa-dozAt vinASaH syAt Silpinam tat na dApayet /
   dāpayec śilpidoṣāt tat saṃskārārthaṃ yad arpitam // K_604 //	dApayet Silpi-dozAt tat saMskAra-arTam yat arpitam // K_604 //
   svalpenāpi ca yat karma naṣṭaṃ ced bhṛtakasya tat /	su-alpena-api ca yat karma nazwam ced BRtakasya tat /
   paryāptaṃ ditsatas tasya vinaśyet tad agṛhṇataḥ // K_605 //	paryAptam ditsataH tasya vinaSyet tat agRhNataH // K_605 //
   yadi tat kāryam uddiśya kālaṃ pariniyamya vā /	yadi tat kAryam uddiSya kAlam pariniyamya vA /
   yācito 'rdhakṛte tasminn aprāpte na tu dāpyate // K_606 //	yAcitaH arDa-kRte tasmin aprApte na tu dApyate // K_606 //
   prāptakāle kṛte kārye na dadyād yācito 'pi san /	prApta-kAle kRte kArye na dadyAt yAcitaH api san /
   tasmin naṣṭe vāpi grahītā mūlyam āharet // K_607 //	tasmin nazwe vA-api grahItA mUlyam Aharet // K_607 //
   yācyamāno na dadyād vā dāpyas tat sodayaṃ bhavet // K_608 //	yAcyamAnaH na dadyAt vA dApyaH tat sa-udayam Bavet // K_608 //
   atha kāryavipattis tu tasyaiva svāmino bhavet /	aTa kArya-vipattiH tu tasya-eva svAminaH Bavet /
   aprāpte vai sa kāle tu dāpyas tv ardhakṛte 'pi tat // K_609 //	aprApte vE sa kAle tu dApyaH tu arDa-kRte api tat // K_609 //
   yo yācitakam ādāya na dadyāt pratiyācitaḥ /	yaH yAcitakam AdAya na dadyAt pratiyAcitaH /
   sa nigṛhya balād dāpyo daṇḍyaś ca na dadāti yaḥ // K_610 //	sa nigRhya balAt dApyaH daNxyaH ca na dadAti yaH // K_610 //
   anumārgeṇa kāryeṣu anyasmin vacanān mama /	anumArgeNa kAryezu anyasmin vacanAt mama /
   dadyās tvam iti yo dattaḥ sa ihānvādhir ucyate // K_611 //	dadyAH tvam iti yaH dattaH saH iha-anvADiH ucyate // K_611 //
   [asvāmivikrayaḥ]	[asvAmi-vikrayaH]
   asvāmivikrayaṃ dānam ādhiṃ ca vinivartayet // K_612 //	asvAmi-vikrayam dAnam ADim ca vinivartayet // K_612 //
   abhiyoktā dhanaṃ kuryāt prathamaṃ jñātibhiḥ svakam /	aBiyoktA Danam kuryAt praTamam jQAtiBiH svakam /
   paścād ātmaviśudhyarthaṃ krayaṃ ketā svabandhubhiḥ // K_613 //	paScAt Atma-viSuDi-arTam krayam ketA sva-banDuBiH // K_613 //
   nāṣṭikas tu prakurvīta tad dhanaṃ jñātṛbhiḥ svakam /	nAzwikaH tu prakurvIta tat Danam jQAtRBiH svakam /
   adattatyaktavikrītaṃ kṛtvā svaṃ labhate dhanam // K_614 //	adatta-tyakta-vikrItam kRtvA svam laBate Danam // K_614 //
   prakāśaṃ vā krayaṃ kuryān mūlaṃ vāpi samarpayet /	prakASam vA krayam kuryAt mUlam vA-api samarpayet /
   mūlānayanakālas tu deyo yojanasaṃkhyayā // K_615 //	mUla-Anayana-kAlaH tu deyaH yojana-saMKyayA // K_615 //
   prakāśaṃ ca krayaṃ kuryāt sādhubhir jñātibhiḥ svakaiḥ /	prakASam ca krayam kuryAt sADuBiH jQAtiBiH svakEH /
   na tatrānyā kriyā proktā daivikī na ca mānuṣī // K_616 //	na tatra-anyA kriyA proktA dEvikI na ca mAnuzI // K_616 //
   yadā mūlam upanyasya punar vādī krayaṃ vadet /	yadA mUlam upanyasya punar vAdI krayam vadet /
   āharen mūlam evāsau na krayeṇa prayojanam // K_617 //	Aharet mUlam eva-asO na krayeNa prayojanam // K_617 //
   asamāhāryamūlas tu krayam eva viśodhayet /	asamAhArya-mUlaH tu krayam eva viSoDayet /
   viśodhite kraye rājñā na vaktavyaḥ sa kiṃcana // K_618 //	viSoDite kraye rAjQA na vaktavyaH sa kiMcana // K_618 //
   anupasthāpayan mūlaṃ krayaṃ vāpy aviśodhayan /	anupasTApayan mUlam krayam vA-api aviSoDayan /
   yathābhiyogaṃ dhanine dhanaṃ dāpyo damaṃ ca saḥ // K_619 //	yaTA-aBiyogam Danine Danam dApyaH damam ca saH // K_619 //
   yadi svaṃ naiva kurute jñātibhir nāṣṭiko dhanam /	yadi svam na-eva kurute jQAtiBiH nAzwikaH Danam /
   prasaṅgavinivṛttyarthaṃ coravaddaṇḍam arhati // K_620 //	prasaFga-vinivRtti-arTam cora-vat-daNxam arhati // K_620 //
   vaniṅvīthīparigataṃ vijñātaṃ rājapuruṣaiḥ /	vaniFvITI-parigatam vijQAtam rAja-puruzEH /
   avijñātāśrayāt krītaṃ vikretā yatra vā mṛtaḥ // K_621 //	avijQAta-ASrayAt krItam vikretA yatra vA mRtaH // K_621 //
   svāmī datvārdhamūlyaṃ tu pragṛhṇīta svaka dhanam /	svAmI datvA-arDa-mUlyam tu pragRhNIta svaka Danam /
   ardhaṃ dvayor apahṛtaṃ tatra syād vyavahārataḥ // K_622 //	arDam dvayoH apahRtam tatra syAt vyavahArataH // K_622 //
   avijñātakrayo doṣas tathā cāparipālanam /	avijQAta-krayaH dozaH taTA ca-aparipAlanam /
   etad dvayaṃ samākhyātaṃ dravyahānikaraṃ buddhaiḥ // K_623 //	etat dvayam samAKyAtam dravya-hAni-karam budDEH // K_623 //
   [sambhūyasamutthānam]	[samBUyasamutTAnam-]
   samavetās tu ye kecic śalpino vaṇijo 'pi vā /	samavetAH tu ye kecid SalpinaH vaNijaH api vA /
   avibhajya pṛthagbhūtaiḥ prāptaṃ tatra phalaṃ samam // K_624 //	aviBajya pRTak-BUtEH prAptam tatra Palam samam // K_624 //
   bhāṇḍapiṇḍavyayoddhāra- bhārasārārthavīkṣaṇam /	BANxa-piNxa-vyayodDAra BArasAra-arTa-vIkzaNam /
   kuryus te 'vyabhicāreṇa samayena vyavasthitāḥ // K_625 //	kuryuH te avyaBicAreNa samayena vyavasTitAH // K_625 //
   prayogaṃ kurvate ye tu hemadhānyarasādinā /	prayogam kurvate ye tu hema-DAnya-rasa-AdinA /
   samanyūnādhikair aṃśair lābhas teṣāṃ tathāvidhaḥ // K_626 //	sama-nyUna-aDikEH aMSEH lABaH tezAm taTAviDaH // K_626 //
   bahūnāṃ saṃmato yas tu dadyād eko dhanaṃ naraḥ /	bahUnAm saMmataH yaH tu dadyAt ekaH Danam naraH /
   ṛṇaṃ ca kārayed vāpi sarvair eva kṛtaṃ bhavet // K_627 //	RNam ca kArayet vA-api sarvEH eva kRtam Bavet // K_627 //
   jñātisaṃbandhisuhṛdām ṛṇaṃ deyaṃ sabandhakam /	jQAti-saMbanDi-suhRdAm RNam deyam sa-banDakam /
   anyeṣāṃ lagnakopetaṃ lekhyasākṣiyutaṃ tathā // K_628 //	anyezAm lagnaka-upetam leKya-sAkzi-yutam taTA // K_628 //
   svecchādeyaṃ hiraṇyaṃ tu rasā dhānyaṃ ca sāvidhi /	sva-icCA-deyam hiraNyam tu rasAH DAnyam ca sAviDi /
   deśasthityā pradātavyaṃ grahītavyaṃ tathaiva ca // K_629 //	deSa-sTityA pradAtavyam grahItavyam taTA-eva ca // K_629 //
   samavetais tu yad dattaṃ prārthanīyaṃ tathaiva tat /	samavetEH tu yat dattam prArTanIyam taTA-eva tat /
   na ca yāceta yaḥ kaścil lābhāt sa parihīyate // K_630 //	na ca yAceta yaH kaScid lABAt sa parihIyate // K_630 //
   corataḥ salilād agner dravyaṃ yas tu samāharet /	corataH salilAt agneH dravyam yaH tu samAharet /
   tasyāṃśo daśamo deyaḥ sarvavādeṣv ayaṃ vidhiḥ // K_631 //	tasya-aMSaH daSamaH deyaH sarva-vAdezu ayam viDiH // K_631 //
   śikṣakābhijñakuśalā ācāryaś ceti śilpinaḥ /	Sikzaka-aBijQa-kuSalAH AcAryaH ca-iti SilpinaH /
   ekadvitricaturbhāgān hareyus te yathottaram // K_632 //	eka-dvi-tri-catur-BAgAn hareyuH te yaTottaram // K_632 //
   pararāṣṭrād dhanaṃ yat syāc cauraiḥ svāmyājñayāhṛtam /	para-rAzwrAt Danam yat syAt cOrEH svAmi-AjQayA-AhRtam /
   rājño daśāṃśam uddhṛtya vibhajeran yathāvidhi // K_633 //	rAjQaH daSa-aMSam udDRtya viBajeran yaTAviDi // K_633 //
   corāṇāṃ mukhyabhūtas tu caturo 'ṃśāṃs tato haret /	corANAm muKya-BUtaH tu caturaH aMSAn tatas haret /
   śūro 'ṃśāṃs trīn samartho dvau śoṣās tv ekaikam eva ca // K_634 //	SUraH aMSAn trIn samarTaH dvO SozAH tu ekEkam eva ca // K_634 //
   teṣāṃ cet prasṛtānāṃ yo grahaṇaṃ samavāpnuyāt /	tezAm ced prasRtAnAm yaH grahaNam samavApnuyAt /
   tanmokṣaṇārthaṃ yad dattaṃ vaheyus te yathāṃśataḥ // K_635 //	tad-mokzaNa-arTam yat dattam vaheyuH te yaTA-aMSataH // K_635 //
   nartakānām eṣa eva dharmaḥ sadbhir udāhṛtaḥ /	nartakAnAm ezaH eva DarmaH sadBiH udAhRtaH /
   tālajño labhate hy ardhaṃ gāyanās tu samāṃśinaḥ /	tAla-jQaH laBate hi arDam gAyanAH tu sama-aMSinaH /
   pramukhā dvyaṃśam arhanti so 'yaṃ saṃbhūya kurvatām // K_636 //	pramuKAH dvi-aMSam arhanti saH ayam saMBUya kurvatAm // K_636 //
   vaṇijāṃ karṣakāṇāṃ ca corāṇāṃ śilpināṃ tathā /	vaNijAm karzakANAm ca corANAm SilpinAm taTA /
   aniyamyāṃśakartṝṇāṃ sarveṣām eṣa nirṇayaḥ // K_637 //	aniyamya-aMSa-kartLNAm sarvezAm eza nirNayaH // K_637 //
   [dattānapākarma dattāpradānikaṃ vā]	[dattAn-apAkarma datta-apradAnikam vA]
   vikrayaṃ caiva dānaṃ ca na neyāḥ syur anicchavaḥ /	vikrayam ca-eva dAnam ca na neyAH syuH anicCavaH /
   dārāḥ putrāś ca sarvasvam ātmanaiva tu yojayet // K_638 //	dArAH putrAH ca sarva-svam AtmanA-eva tu yojayet // K_638 //
   āpatkāle tu kartavyaṃ dānaṃ vikraya eva vā /	Apad-kAle tu kartavyam dAnam vikrayaH eva vA /
   anyathā na pravarteta iti śāstraviniścayaḥ // K_639 //	anyaTA na pravarteta iti SAstra-viniScayaH // K_639 //
   sarvasvagṛhavarjaṃ tu kuṭumbabharaṇādhikam /	sarva-sva-gRha-varjam tu kuwumba-BaraNa-aDikam /
   yad dravyaṃ tat svakaṃ deyam adeyaṃ syād ato 'nyathā // K_640 //	yat dravyam tat svakam deyam adeyam syAt atas anyaTA // K_640 //
   ataś ca sutadārāṇāṃ vaśitvaṃ tv anuśāsane /	atas ca suta-dArANAm vaSitvam tu anuSAsane /
   vikraye caiva dāne ca vaśitvaṃ na sute pituḥ // K_641 //	vikraye ca-eva dAne ca vaSitvam na sute pituH // K_641 //
   svecchayā yaḥ pratiśrutya brāhmaṇāya pratigraham /	sva-icCayA yaH pratiSrutya brAhmaNAya pratigraham /
   na dadyād ṛṇava dāpyaḥ prāpnuyāt pūrvasāhasam // K_642 //	na dadyAt RNava dApyaH prApnuyAt pUrva-sAhasam // K_642 //
   pratiśrutasyādānena dattasyācchādanena ca /	pratiSrutasya-AdAnena dattasya-AcCAdanena ca /
   kalpakoṭiśataṃ martyas tiryagyonau ca jāyate // K_643 //	kalpa-kowi-Satam martyaH tiryagyonO ca jAyate // K_643 //
   avijñātopalabdhyarthaṃ dānaṃ yatra nirūpitam /	avijQAta-upalabDi-arTam dAnam yatra nirUpitam /
   upalabdhikriyālabdhaṃ sā bhṛtiḥ parikīrtitā // K_644 //	upalabDi-kriyA-labDam sA BRtiH parikIrtitAH // K_644 //
   bhayatrāṇāya rakṣārthaṃ tathā kāryaprasādhanāt /	Baya-trANAya rakzA-arTam taTA kArya-prasADanAt /
   anena vidhinā labdhaṃ vidyāt pratyupakārataḥ // K_645 //	anena viDinA labDam vidyAt pratyupakArataH // K_645 //
   prāṇasaṃśayam āpannaṃ yo mām uttārayed itaḥ /	prANa-saMSayam Apannam yaH mAm uttArayet itas /
   sarvasvaṃ tasya dāsyāmīty ukte 'pi na tathā bhavet // K_646 //	sarva-svam tasya dAsyAmi-iti ukte api na taTA Bavet // K_646 //
   kāmakrodhāsvatantrārta- klībonmattapramohitaiḥ /	kAma-kroDa-asvatantra-Arta klIba-unmatta-pramohitEH /
   vyatyāsaparihāsāc ca yad dattaṃ tat punar haret // K_647 //	vyatyAsa-parihAsAt ca yat dattam tat punar haret // K_647 //
   yā tu kāryasya siddhyartham utkocā syāt pratiśrutā /	yA tu kAryasya sidDi-arTam utkocA syAt pratiSrutAH /
   tasminn api pasiddhe 'rthe na deyā syāt kathaṃcana // K_648 //	tasmin api pasidDe arTe na deyA syAt kaTaMcana // K_648 //
   atha prāg eva dattā syāt pratidāpyas tathā balāt /	aTa prAk eva dattA syAt pratidApyaH taTA balAt /
   daṇḍaṃ caikādaśaguṇam āhur gārgīyamānavāḥ // K_649 //	daNxam ca-ekAdaSaguNam AhuH gArgIya-mAnavAH // K_649 //
   stenasāhasikodvṛtta- pārajāyikaśaṃsanāt /	stena-sAhasika-udvRtta pArajAyika-SaMsanAt /
   darśanād vṛttanaṣṭasya tathāsatyapravartanāt // K_650 //	darSanAt vRtta-nazwasya taTA-asatya-pravartanAt // K_650 //
   prāptam etais tu yat kiṃcit tad utkocākhyam ucyate /	prAptam etEH tu yat kiMcid tat utkoca-AKyam ucyate /
   na dātā tatra daṇḍyaḥ syān madhyasthaś caiva doṣabhāk // K_651 //	na dAtA tatra daNxyaH syAt maDyasTaH ca-eva doza-BAj // K_651 //
   niyukto yas tu kāryeṣu sa ced utkocam āpnuyāt /	niyuktaH yaH tu kAryezu sa ced utkocam ApnuyAt /
   sa dāpyas taddhanaṃ kṛtsnaṃ damaś caikādaśādhikam // K_652 //	sa dApyaH tad-Danam kRtsnam damaH ca-ekAdaSa-aDikam // K_652 //
   aniyuktas tu kāryārtham utkocaṃ yam avāpnuyāt /	aniyuktaH tu kArya-arTam utkocam yam avApnuyAt /
   kṛtapratyupakārārthas tasya doṣo na vidyate // K_653 //	kRta-pratyupakAra-arTaH tasya dozaH na vidyate // K_653 //
   svasthenārtena vā dattaṃ śrāvritaṃ dharmakāraṇāt /	svasTena-Artena vA dattam SrAvritam Darma-kAraNAt /
   adattvā tu mṛte dāpyas tatsuto nātra saṃśayaḥ // K_654 //	adattvA tu mRte dApyaH tad-sutaH na-atra saMSayaH // K_654 //
   yogādhamanavikrītaṃ yogadānapatigraham /	yoga-ADamana-vikrItam yoga-dAna-pati-graham /
   yasya vāpy upadhiṃ paśyet tat sarvaṃ vinivartayet // K_655 //	yasya vA-api upaDim paSyet tat sarvam vinivartayet // K_655 //
   bhṛtāvaniścitāyāṃ tu daśabhāgam avāpnuyāt /	BRta-avaniScitAyAm tu daSa-BAgam avApnuyAt /
   lābhagovīryasasyānāṃ vaṇiggopakṛṣīvalāḥ // K_656 //	lABa-go-vIrya-sasyAnAm vaNiggopa-kRzIvalAH // K_656 //
   [vetanasyānapākarma]	[vetanasya-anapAkarma]
   karmārambhaṃ tu yaḥ kṛtvā siddhaṃ naiva tu kārayet /	karma-AramBam tu yaH kRtvA sidDam na-eva tu kArayet /
   balāt kārayitavyo 'sau akurvan daṇḍam arhati // K_657 //	balAt kArayitavyaH asO akurvan daNxam arhati // K_657 //
   vighnayan vāhako dāpyaḥ prasthāne dviguṇāṃ bhṛtim // K_658 //	viGnayan vAhakaH dApyaH prasTAne dviguNAm BRtim // K_658 //
   na tu dāpyo hṛtaṃ corair dagdhamūḍhaṃ jalena vā // K_659 //	na tu dApyaH hRtam corEH dagDa-mUXam jalena vA // K_659 //
   tyajet pathi sahāyaṃ yaḥ śrāntaṃ rogārtam eva vā /	tyajet paTi sahAyam yaH SrAntam roga-Artam eva vA /
   prāpnuyāt sāhasaṃ pūrvaṃ grāme tryaham apālayan // K_660 //	prApnuyAt sAhasam pUrvam grAme tri-aham apAlayan // K_660 //
   yadā tu pathi tadbhāṇḍam āsidhyeta hriyeta vā /	yadA tu paTi tat-BANxam AsiDyeta hriyeta vA /
   yāvān adhvā gatas tena prāpnuyāt tāvatīṃ bhṛtim // K_661 //	yAvAn aDvA gataH tena prApnuyAt tAvatIm BRtim // K_661 //
   hastyaśvagokharoṣṭrādīn gṛhītvā bhāṭakena yaḥ /	hasti-aSva-go-Kara-uzwra-AdIn gRhItvA BAwakena yaH /
   nārpayet kṛtakṛtyārthaḥ sa tu dāpyaḥ sabhāṭakam // K_662 //	na-arpayet kRtakRtya-arTaH sa tu dApyaH sa-BAwakam // K_662 //
   gṛhavāryāpaṇādīṇi gṛhītvā bhāṭakena yaḥ /	gRha-vAri-ApaNa-AdINi gRhItvA BAwakena yaH /
   svāmine nārpayed yāvat tāvad dāpyaḥ sabhāṭakam // K_663 //	svAmine na-arpayet yAvat tAvat dApyaH sa-BAwakam // K_663 //
   [svāmipālavivādaḥ]	[sva-Ami-pAla-vivAdaH]
   kṣetrārāmavivīteṣu gṛheṣu paśuvāṭiṣu /	kzetra-ArAma-vivItezu gRhezu paSu-vAwizu /
   grahaṇaṃ tatpraviṣṭānāṃ tāḍanaṃ vā bṛhaspatiḥ // K_664 //	grahaNam tad-pravizwAnAm tAxanam vA bRhaspatiH // K_664 //
   adhamottamamadhyānāṃ paśūnāṃ caiva tāḍane /	aDama-uttama-maDyAnAm paSUnAm ca-eva tAxane /
   svāmī tu vivaded yatra daṇḍaṃ tatra prakalpayet // K_665 //	svAmI tu vivadet yatra daNxam tatra prakalpayet // K_665 //
   ajāteṣv eva sasyeṣu kuryād āvaraṇaṃ mahat /	ajAtezu eva sasyezu kuryAt AvaraNam mahat /
   duḥkheneha nivāryante labdhasvādurasā mṛgāḥ // K_666 //	duHKena-iha nivAryante labDa-svAdu-rasAH mRgAH // K_666 //
   dāpayet paṇapādaṃ gāṃ dvau pādau mahiṣīṃ tathā /	dApayet paNa-pAdam gAm dvO pAdO mahizIm taTA /
   tathājāvikavatsānāṃ pādo daṇḍaḥ prakīrtitaḥ // K_667 //	taTA-aja-Avika-vatsAnAm pAdaH daNxaH prakIrtitaH // K_667 //
   [samayasyānapākarma saṃvidvyatikramo vā]	[samayasya-anapAkarma saMvid-vyatikramaH vA]
   samūhināṃ tu yo dharmas tena dharmeṇa te sadā /	samUhinAm tu yaH DarmaH tena DarmeNa te sadA /
   prakuryuḥ sarvakarmāṇi svadharmeṣu vyavasthitāḥ // K_668 //	prakuryuH sarva-karmANi svaDarmezu vyavasTitAH // K_668 //
   avirodhena dharmasya nirgataṃ rājaśāsanam /	aviroDena Darmasya nirgatam rAja-SAsanam /
   tasyaivācaraṇaṃ pūrvaṃ kartavyaṃ tu nṛpājñayā // K_669 //	tasya-eva-AcaraNam pUrvam kartavyam tu nRpa-AjQayA // K_669 //
   rājapravartitān dharmān yo naro nānupālayet /	rAja-pravartitAn DarmAn yaH naraH na-anupAlayet /
   garhyaḥ sa pāpo daṇḍyaś ca lopayan rājaśāsanam // K_670 //	garhyaH sa pApaH daNxyaH ca lopayan rAja-SAsanam // K_670 //
   yuktiyuktaṃ ca yo hanyād vaktur yo 'navakāśadaḥ /	yukti-yuktam ca yaH hanyAt vaktuH yaH anavakASa-daH /
   ayuktaṃ caiva yo brūte sa dāpyaḥ pūrvasāhasam // K_671 //	ayuktam ca-eva yaH brUte sa dApyaH pUrva-sAhasam // K_671 //
   sāhasī bhedakārī ca gaṇadravyavināśakaḥ /	sAhasI Beda-kArI ca gaNa-dravya-vinASakaH /
   ucchedyāḥ sarva evaite vikhyāpyaivaṃ nṛpe bhṛguḥ // K_672 //	ucCedyAH sarve eva-ete viKyApya-evam nRpe BRguH // K_672 //
   ekapātre ca vā paṅktyāṃ saṃbhoktā yasya yo bhavet /	eka-pAtre ca vA paFktyAm saMBoktA yasya yaH Bavet /
   akurvaṃs tat tathā daṇḍyas tasya doṣam adarśayan // K_673 //	akurvan tat taTA daNxyaH tasya dozam adarSayan // K_673 //
   gaṇam uddiśya yat kiṃcit kṛtvarṇaṃ bhakṣitaṃ bhavet /	gaNam uddiSya yat kiMcid kRtvA-RNam Bakzitam Bavet /
   ātmārthaṃ viniyuktaṃ vā deyaṃ tair eva tad bhavet // K_674 //	Atma-arTam viniyuktam vA deyam tEH eva tat Bavet // K_674 //
   gaṇānāṃ śreṇivargāṇāṃ gatāḥ syur ye tu madhyatām /	gaNAnAm SreNi-vargANAm gatAH syuH ye tu maDya-tAm /
   prāktanasya dhanarṇasya samāṃśāḥ sarva eva te // K_675 //	prAktanasya Dana-RNasya sama-aMSAH sarve eva te // K_675 //
   tathaiva bhojyavaibhājya- dānadharmakriyāsu ca /	taTA-eva Bojya-vEBAjya dAna-Darma-kriyAsu ca /
   samūhastho 'ṃśabhāgī syāt pragatas tv aṃśabhāṅ na tu // K_676 //	samUha-sTaH aMSa-BAgI syAt pragataH tu aMSa-BAj na tu // K_676 //
   yat taiḥ prāptaṃ rakṣitaṃ vā gaṇārthe vā ṛṇaṃ kṛtam /	yat tEH prAptam rakzitam vA gaNa-arTe vE RNam kRtam /
   rājaprasādalabdhaṃ ca sarveṣām eva tatsamam // K_677 //	rAja-prasAda-labDam ca sarvezAm eva tad-samam // K_677 //
   [naigamādisaṃjñālakṣaṇam]	[nEgama-Adi-saMjQA-lakzaNam]
   nānāpaurasamūhas tu naigamaḥ parikīrtitaḥ /	nAnA-pOra-samUhaH tu nEgamaH parikIrtitaH /
   nānāyudhadharā vrātāḥ samavetāḥ prakīrtitāḥ // K_678 //	nAnA-AyuDa-DarAH vrAtAH samavetAH prakIrtitAH // K_678 //
   samūho vaṇijādīnāṃ pūgaḥ saṃparikīrtitaḥ /	samUhaH vaNija-AdInAm pUgaH saMparikIrtitaH /
   pravrajyāvasitā ye tu pāṣaṇḍāḥ parikīrtitāḥ // K_679 //	pravrajyA-vasitAH ye tu pAzaNxAH parikIrtitAH // K_679 //
   brāhmaṇānāṃ samūhas tu gaṇaḥ saṃparikīrtitaḥ /	brAhmaNAnAm samUhaH tu gaNaH saMparikIrtitaH /
   śilpopajīvino ye tu śilpinaḥ parikīrtitāḥ // K_680 //	Silpa-upajIvinaH ye tu SilpinaH parikIrtitAH // K_680 //
   ārhatasaugatānāṃ tu samūhaḥ saṅgha ucyate /	Arhata-sOgatAnAm tu samUhaH saFGaH ucyate /
   cāṇḍālaśvapacādīnāṃ samūho gulma ucyate // K_681 //	cANxAla-Svapaca-AdInAm samUhaH gulmaH ucyate // K_681 //
   gaṇapāṣaṇḍapūgāś ca vrātāś ca śreṇayas tathā /	gaNa-pAzaNxa-pUgAH ca vrAtAH ca SreNayaH taTA /
   samūhasthāś ca ye cānye vargākhyās te bṛhaspatiḥ // K_682 //	samUha-sTAH ca ye ca-anye varga-AKyAH te bRhaspatiH // K_682 //
   [krayakikrayānuśayaḥ krīsvānuśayo vikrīye saṃpradānaṃ vā]	[kraya-kikraya-anuSayaH krIsva-anuSayaH vikrIye saMpradAnam vA]
   krītvā prāptaṃ na gṛhṇīyād yo na dadyād adūṣitam /	krItvA prAptam na gRhNIyAt yaH na dadyAt adUzitam /
   sa mūlyād daśamaṃ bhāgaṃ dattvā svadravyam āpnuyāt // K_683 //	sa mUlyAt daSamam BAgam dattvA sva-dravyam ApnuyAt // K_683 //
   aprāpte 'rthakriyākāle kṛte naiva pradāpayet /	aprApte arTa-kriyA-kAle kRte na-eva pradApayet /
   evaṃ dharmo daśāhāt tu parato 'nuśayo na tu // K_684 //	evam DarmaH daSa-ahAt tu paratas anuSayaH na tu // K_684 //
   bhūmer daśāhe vikretur āyas tatkretur eva ca /	BUmeH daSa-ahe vikretuH AyaH tad-kretuH eva ca /
   dvādaśāhaḥ sapiṇḍānām api cālpam ataḥ param // K_685 //	dvAdaSa-ahaH sapiNxAnAm api ca-alpam atas param // K_685 //
   krītvānuśayavān paṇyaṃ tyajed dohyādi yo naraḥ /	krItvA-anuSayavAn paNyam tyajet dohya-Adi yaH naraH /
   aduṣṭam eva kāle tu sa mūlyād daśamaṃ vahet // K_686 //	aduzwam eva kAle tu sa mUlyAt daSamam vahet // K_686 //
   krītvā gacchann anuśayaṃ krayī hastam upāgate /	krItvA gacCan anuSayam krayI hastam upAgate /
   ṣaḍbhāgaṃ tatra mūlyasya dattvā krītaṃ tyajed budhaḥ // K_687 //	zaz-BAgam tatra mUlyasya dattvA krItam tyajet buDaH // K_687 //
   avijñātaṃ tu yat krītaṃ duṣṭaṃ paścād vibhāvitam /	avijQAtam tu yat krItam duzwam paScAt viBAvitam /
   krītaṃ tat svāmine deyaṃ kāle ced anyathā na tu // K_688 //	krItam tat svAmine deyam kAle ced anyaTA na tu // K_688 //
   nirdoṣaṃ darśayitvā tu yaḥ sadoṣaṃ prayacchati /	nirdozam darSayitvA tu yaH sa-dozam prayacCati /
   mūlyaṃ tad dviguṇaṃ dāpyo vinayaṃ tāvad eva ca // K_689 //	mUlyam tat dviguNam dApyaH vinayam tAvat eva ca // K_689 //
   upahanyeta vā paṇyaṃ dahyetāpahriyeta vā /	upahanyeta vA paNyam dahyeta-apahriyeta vA /
   vikretur eva so 'nartho vikrīyāsaṃprayacchataḥ // K_690 //	vikretuH eva saH anarTaH vikrIya-asaMprayacCataH // K_690 //
   dīyamānaṃ na gṛhṇāti krīta paṇyaṃ ca yaḥ krayī /	dIyamAnam na gRhNAti krIta paNyam ca yaH krayI /
   vikrītaṃ ca tad anyatra vikretā nāparādhruyāt // K_691 //	vikrItam ca tat anyatra vikretA na-aparADruyAt // K_691 //
   mattonmattena vikrītaṃ hīnamūlyaṃ bhayena vā /	matta-unmattena vikrItam hIna-mUlyam Bayena vA /
   asvatantreṇa mugdhena tyājyaṃ tasya punar bhavet // K_692 //	asvatantreNa mugDena tyAjyam tasya punar Bavet // K_692 //
   tryahaṃ dohyaṃ parīkṣeta patrcāhad vāhyam eva tu /	tri-aham dohyam parIkzeta patrca-ahat vAhyam eva tu /
   muktāvajrapravālānāṃ saptāhaṃ syāt pravīkṣaṇam // K_693 //	muktA-vajra-pravAlAnAm sapta-aham syAt pravIkzaNam // K_693 //
   dvipadām ardhamāsaṃ tu puṃsāṃ tad dviguṇaṃ striyāḥ /	dvipadAm arDa-mAsam tu puMsAm tat dviguNam striyAH /
   daśāhaṃ sarvabījānām ekāhaṃ lohavāsasām // K_694 //	daSa-aham sarva-bIjAnAm eka-aham loha-vAsasAm // K_694 //
   ato 'rvākpaṇyadoṣas tu yadi saṃjāyate kvacit /	atas arvAk-paNya-dozaH tu yadi saMjAyate kvacid /
   vikretuḥ pratideyaṃ tat kretā mūlyam avāpnuyāt // K_695 //	vikretuH pratideyam tat kretA mUlyam avApnuyAt // K_695 //
   paribhuktaṃ tu yad vāsaḥ kliṣṭarūpaṃ malīmasam /	pariBuktam tu yat vAsaH klizwa-rUpam malImasam /
   sadoṣam api tat krītaṃ viketur na bhavet punaḥ // K_696 //	sa-dozam api tat krItam viketuH na Bavet punar // K_696 //
   sādhāraṇaṃ tu yat krītaṃ naiko dadyān narādhamaḥ /	sADAraNam tu yat krItam na-ekaH dadyAt nara-aDamaH /
   nādadyān na ca gṛhṇīyād vikrīyāc ca na caiva hi // K_697 //	na-AdadyAt na ca gRhNIyAt vikrIyAt ca na ca-eva hi // K_697 //
   krītvā mūlyena yat paṇyaṃ duṣkrītaṃ manyate krayī /	krItvA mUlyena yat paNyam duzkrItam manyate krayI /
   vikretuḥ pratideyaṃ tat tasminn evāhnyavīkṣitam // K_698 //	vikretuH pratideyam tat tasmin eva-ahni-avIkzitam // K_698 //
   dvitīye 'hni dadat kretā mūlyāt tryaṃśāṃśam āharet /	dvitIye ahni dadat kretA mUlyAt tri-aMSa-aMSam Aharet /
   dviguṇaṃ tṛtīye 'hni parataḥ kretur eva tat // K_699 //	dviguNam tRtIye ahni paratas kretuH eva tat // K_699 //
   dravyasvaṃ pañcadhā kṛtvā tribhāgo mūlyam ucyate /	dravya-svam paQcaDA kRtvA tri-BAgaH mUlyam ucyate /
   lābhaś caturtho bhāgaḥ syāt pañcamaḥ satyam ucyate // K_700 //	lABaH caturTaH BAgaH syAt paQcamaH satyam ucyate // K_700 //
   sandhiś ca parivṛttiś ca viṣamā vā tribhogataḥ /	sanDiH ca parivRttiH ca vizamAH vA tri-BogataH /
   ājñayāpi krayaś cāpi daśābdaṃ vinivartayet // K_701 //	AjQayA-api krayaH ca-api daSa-abdam vinivartayet // K_701 //
   jñātyādīn ananujñāpya samīpasthānaninditān /	jQAti-AdIn ananujQApya samIpa-sTAn-aninditAn /
   krayavikrayadharmo 'pi bhūmer nāstīti nirṇayaḥ // K_702 //	kraya-vikraya-DarmaH api BUmeH na-asti-iti nirNayaH // K_702 //
   svagrāme daśarātraṃ syād anyagrāme tripakṣakam /	sva-grAme daSa-rAtram syAt anya-grAme tri-pakzakam /
   rāṣṭrāntareṣu ṣaṇmāsaṃ bhāṣābhede tu vatsaram // K_703 //	rAzwra-antarezu zaz-mAsam BAzA-Bede tu vatsaram // K_703 //
   palāyite tu karade karapratibhuvā saha /	palAyite tu kara-de kara-pratiBuvA saha /
   karārthaṃ karadakṣetraṃ vikrīṇīyuḥ sabhāsadaḥ // K_704 //	kara-arTam karada-kzetram vikrINIyuH saBAsadaH // K_704 //
   samavetais tu sāmantair abhijñaiḥ pāpabhīrubhiḥ /	samavetEH tu sAmantEH aBijQEH pApa-BIruBiH /
   kṣetrārāmagṛhādīnāṃ dvipadāṃ ca catuṣpadām // K_705 //	kzetra-ArAma-gRha-AdInAm dvipadAm ca catuzpadAm // K_705 //
   kalpitaṃ mūlyam ity āhur bhāgaṃ kṛtvā tad aṣṭadhā /	kalpitam mUlyam iti AhuH BAgam kRtvA tat azwaDA /
   ekabhāgātiriktaṃ vā hīnaṃ vānucitaṃ smṛtam // K_706 //	eka-BAga-atiriktam vA hInam vA-anucitam smRtam // K_706 //
   samāḥ śatam atīte 'pi sarvaṃ tad vinivartate /	samAH Satam atIte api sarvam tat vinivartate /
   krayavikrayaṇe krayyaṃ yan mūlyaṃ dharmato 'rhati // K_707 //	kraya-vikrayaNe krayyam yat mUlyam DarmataH arhati // K_707 //
   tat turye pañcame ṣaṣṭe saptame 'ṃśe 'ṣṭame 'pi vā /	tat turye paQcame zazwe saptame aMSe azwame api vA /
   hīne yadi vinirvṛtte krayavikrāyaṇe sati // K_708 //	hIne yadi vinirvRtte kraya-vikrAyaNe sati // K_708 //
   hīnamūlyaṃ tu tat sarvaṃ kṛtam apy akṛtaṃ bhavet /	hIna-mUlyam tu tat sarvam kRtam api akRtam Bavet /
   uktād alpatare hīne krayo naiva praduṣyati // K_709 //	uktAt alpatare hIne krayaH na-eva praduzyati // K_709 //
   tenāpy aṃśena hīyeta mūlyataḥ krayavikraye /	tena-api aMSena hIyeta mUlyataH kraya-vikraye /
   katam apy akṛtaṃ prāhur anye dharmavido janāḥ // K_710 //	katam api akRtam prAhuH anye Darma-vidaH janAH // K_710 //
   ardhādhike krayaḥ sidhyed uktalābho daśādhikaḥ /	arDa-aDike krayaH siDyet ukta-lABaH daSa-aDikaH /
   avakrayas tribhāgena sadya eva rucikrayaḥ // K_711 //	avakrayaH tri-BAgena sadyas eva ruci-krayaH // K_711 //
   mūlyāt svalpapradāne 'pi krayasiddhiḥ kṛtā bhavet /	mUlyAt su-alpa-pradAne api kraya-sidDiH kRtA Bavet /
   cakravṛddyāṃ pradātavyaṃ deyaṃ tat samayād ṛte // K_712 //	cakravRddyAm pradAtavyam deyam tat samayAt Rte // K_712 //
   [abhyupetyāśuśrūṣā]	[aByupetya-aSuSrUzA]
   yas tu na grāhayec śilpaṃ karmāṇy anyāni kārayet /	yaH tu na grAhayet Silpam karmANi anyAni kArayet /
   prāpnuyāt sāhasaṃ pūrvaṃ tasmāc śiṣyo nivartate // K_713 //	prApnuyAt sAhasam pUrvam tasmAt SizyaH nivartate // K_713 //
   śikṣito 'pi śritaṃ kāmam antevāsī samācaret /	SikzitaH api Sritam kAmam antevAsI samAcaret /
   tatra karma ca yat kuryād ācāryasyaiva tat phalam // K_714 //	tatra karma ca yat kuryAt AcAryasya-eva tat Palam // K_714 //
   svatantrasyātmano dānād dāsatvaṃ dāravad bhṛguḥ /	svatantrasya-AtmanaH dAnAt dAsa-tvam dAra-vat BRguH /
   triṣu varṇeṣu vijñeyaṃ dāsyaṃ viprasya na kvacit // K_715 //	trizu varNezu vijQeyam dAsyam viprasya na kvacid // K_715 //
   varṇānām anulāmyena dāsyaṃ na pratilomataḥ /	varNAnAm anulAmyena dAsyam na pratilomataH /
   rājanyavaiśyaśūdrāṇāṃ tyajatāṃ hi svatantratām // K_716 //	rAjanya-vESya-SUdrANAm tyajatAm hi svatantra-tAm // K_716 //
   samavarṇo 'pi vipraṃ tu dāsatvaṃ naiva kārayet /	samavarNaH api vipram tu dAsa-tvam na-eva kArayet /
   brāhmaṇasya hi dāsatvān nṛpatejo vihanyate // K_717 //	brAhmaNasya hi dAsa-tvAt nRpa-tejaH vihanyate // K_717 //
   kṣatraviśśūdradharmas tu samavarṇe kadācana /	kzatra-viS-SUdra-DarmaH tu sama-varNe kadAcana /
   kārayed dāsakarmāṇi brāhmaṇaṃ na bṛhaspatiḥ // K_718 //	kArayet dAsa-karmANi brAhmaNam na bRhaspatiH // K_718 //
   śīlādhyayanasaṃpanne tadūnaṃ karma kāmataḥ /	SIla-aDyayana-saMpanne tat-Unam karma kAmataH /
   tatrāpi nāśubhaṃ kiṃcit prakurvīta dvijottamaḥ // K_719 //	tatra-api na-aSuBam kiMcid prakurvIta dvijottamaH // K_719 //
   viṇmūtronmārjanaṃ caiva nagnatvaparimardanam /	viz-mUtra-unmArjanam ca-eva nagna-tva-parimardanam /
   prāyo dāsīsutāḥ kuryur gavādigrahaṇaṃ ca yat // K_720 //	prAyas dAsI-sutAH kuryuH gavA-Adi-grahaNam ca yat // K_720 //
   pravrajyāvasitā yatra trayo varṇā dvijādayaḥ /	pravrajyA-vasitAH yatra trayaH varNAH dvija-AdayaH /
   nirvāsaṃ kārayed vipraṃ dāsatvaṃ kṣatraviḍ nṛpaḥ // K_721 //	nirvAsam kArayet vipram dAsa-tvam kzatra-viz nRpaH // K_721 //
   śūdraṃ tu kārayed dāsaṃ krītam akrītam eva vā /	SUdram tu kArayet dAsam krItam akrItam eva vA /
   dāsyāyaiva hi sṛṣṭaḥ sa svayam eva svayam bhuvā // K_722 //	dAsyAya-eva hi sRzwaH sa svayam eva svayam BuvA // K_722 //
   svadāsīṃ yas tu saṃgacchet prasūtā ca bhavet tataḥ /	sva-dAsIm yaH tu saMgacCet prasUtA ca Bavet tatas /
   avekṣya bījaṃ kāryā syān na dāsī sānvayā tu sā // K_723 //	avekzya bIjam kAryA syAt na dAsI sa-anvayA tu sA // K_723 //
   dāsasya tu dhanaṃ yat syāt svāmī tasya prabhuḥ smṛtaḥ /	dAsasya tu Danam yat syAt svAmI tasya praBuH smRtaH /
   prakāśaṃ vikrayād yat tu na svāmī dhanam arhati // K_724 //	prakASam vikrayAt yat tu na svAmI Danam arhati // K_724 //
   dāsenoḍhā svadāsī yā sāpi dāsītvam āpnuyāt /	dAsena-UXA sva-dAsI yA sA-api dAsI-tvam ApnuyAt /
   yasmād bhartā prabhus tasyāḥ svāmyadhīnaḥ prabhur yataḥ // K_725 //	yasmAt BartA praBuH tasyAH svAmi-aDInaH praBuH yatas // K_725 //
   ādadyād brāhmaṇīṃ yas tu cikrīṇīta tathaiva ca /	AdadyAt brAhmaNIm yaH tu cikrINIta taTA-eva ca /
   rājñā tad akṛtaṃ kāryaṃ daṇḍyā syuḥ sarva eva te // K_726 //	rAjQA tat akRtam kAryam daNxyA syuH sarve eva te // K_726 //
   kāmāt tu saṃśritāṃ yas tu dāsīṃ kuryāt kulastriyam /	kAmAt tu saMSritAm yaH tu dAsIm kuryAt kula-striyam /
   saṃkrāmayeta vānyatra daṇḍyas tac cākṛtaṃ bhavet // K_727 //	saMkrAmayeta vA-anyatra daNxyaH tat ca-akRtam Bavet // K_727 //
   bāladhātrīm adāsīṃ ca dāsīm iva bhunakti yaḥ /	bAla-DAtrIm adAsIm ca dAsIm iva Bunakti yaH /
   paricārakapatnīṃ vā prāpnuyāt pūrvasāhasam // K_728 //	paricAraka-patnIm vA prApnuyAt pUrva-sAhasam // K_728 //
   vikrośamānāṃ yo bhaktāṃ dāsīṃ vikretum icchati /	vikroSamAnAm yaH BaktAm dAsIm vikretum icCati /
   anāpadisthaḥ śaktaḥ san prāpnuyād dviśataṃ damam // K_729 //	anApadi-sTaH SaktaH san prApnuyAt dvi-Satam damam // K_729 //
   tavāham iti cātmānaṃ yo 'svatantraḥ prayacchati /	tava-aham iti ca-AtmAnam yaH asvatantraH prayacCati /
   na sa taṃ prāpnuyāt kāmaṃ pūrvasvāmī labheta tam // K_730 //	na sa tam prApnuyAt kAmam pUrva-svAmI laBeta tam // K_730 //
   pravrajyāvasito dāso moktavyaś ca na kenacit /	pravrajyA-vasitaH dAsaH moktavyaH ca na kenacid /
   anākālabhṛto dāsyān mucyate goyugaṃ dadat // K_731 //	anAkAla-BRtaH dAsyAt mucyate go-yugam dadat // K_731 //
   [sīmāvivādaḥ]	[sImA-vivAdaH]
   ādhikyaṃ nyūnatā cāṃśe astināstitvam eva ca /	ADikyam nyUna-tA ca-aMSe astinA-astitvam eva ca /
   abhogabhuktiḥ sīmā ca ṣaṭ bhūvād asya hetavaḥ // K_732 //	aBoga-BuktiH sImA ca zaw BUvAt asya hetavaH // K_732 //
   tasmin bhogaḥ prayoktavyaḥ sarvasākṣiṣu tiṣṭhati /	tasmin BogaH prayoktavyaH sarva-sAkzizu tizWati /
   lekhyārūḍhaś cetaraś ca sākṣī mārgadvayānvitaḥ // K_733 //	leKya-ArUXaH ca-itaraH ca sAkzI mArga-dvaya-anvitaH // K_733 //
   kṣetravāstutaḍāgeṣu kūpopavanasetuṣu /	kzetra-vAstu-taxAgezu kUpa-upavana-setuzu /
   dvayor vivāde sāmantaḥ pratyayaḥ sarvavastuṣu // K_734 //	dvayoH vivAde sAmantaH pratyayaH sarva-vastuzu // K_734 //
   sāmantabhāve 'sāmantaiḥ kuryāt kṣetrādinirṇayam /	sAmanta-BAve asAmantEH kuryAt kzetra-Adi-nirNayam /
   grāmasīmāsu ca tathā tadvan nagaradeśayoḥ // K_735 //	grAma-sImAsu ca taTA tadvat nagara-deSayoH // K_735 //
   grāmo grāmasya sāmantaḥ kṣetraṃ kṣetrasya kīrtitam /	grAmaH grAmasya sAmantaH kzetram kzetrasya kIrtitam /
   gṛhaṃ gṛhasya nirdiṣṭa samantāt parirabhya hi // K_736 //	gRham gRhasya nirdizwa samantAt pariraBya hi // K_736 //
   teṣām abhāve sāmanta- maulavṛddhoddhṛtādayaḥ /	tezAm aBAve sAmanta mOla-vRdDa-udDRta-AdayaH /
   sthāvare ṣaṭprakāre 'pi nātra kāryā vicāraṇā // K_737 //	sTAvare zaz-prakAre api na-atra kAryA vicAraNA // K_737 //
   saṃsaktās tv atha sāmantās tat saṃsaktās tathottarāḥ /	saMsaktAH tu aTa sAmantAH tat saMsaktAH taTA-uttarAH /
   saṃsaktasaktasaṃsaktāḥ padmākārāḥ prakīrtitāḥ // K_738 //	saMsakta-sakta-saMsaktAH padma-AkArAH prakIrtitAH // K_738 //
   svārthasiddhau praduṣṭeṣu sāmanteṣv arthagauravāt /	sva-arTa-sidDO praduzwezu sAmantezu arTa-gOravAt /
   tatsaṃsaktais tu kartavya uddhāro nātra saṃśayaḥ // K_739 //	tad-saMsaktEH tu kartavyaH udDAraH na-atra saMSayaH // K_739 //
   saṃsaktasaktadoṣe tu tatsaṃsaktāḥ prakīrtitāḥ /	saMsakta-sakta-doze tu tad-saMsaktAH prakIrtitAH /
   kartavyā na praduṣṭās tu rājñā dharmaṃ vijānatā // K_740 //	kartavyAH na praduzwAH tu rAjQA Darmam vijAnatA // K_740 //
   nājñānena hi mucyante sāmantā nirṇayaṃ prati /	na-ajQAnena hi mucyante sAmantAH nirNayam prati /
   ajñānoktau daṇḍayitvā punaḥ sīmāṃ vicārayet /	ajQAna-uktO daNxayitvA punar sImAm vicArayet /
   kīrtite yadi bhedaḥ syād daṇḍyās tūttamasāhasam // K_741 //	kIrtite yadi BedaH syAt daNxyAH tu-uttamasAhasam // K_741 //
   tyaktvā duṣṭāṃs tu sāmantān anyān maulādibhiḥ saha /	tyaktvA duzwAn tu sAmantAn anyAn mOla-AdiBiH saha /
   saṃmiśraya kārayet sīmām evaṃ dharmavido viduḥ // K_742 //	saMmiSraya kArayet sImAm evam Darma-vidaH viduH // K_742 //
   ye tatra pūrvaṃ sāmantāḥ paścād deśāntaraṃ gatāḥ /	ye tatra pUrvam sAmantAH paScAt deSa-antaram gatAH /
   tanmūlatvāt tu te maulā ṛṣibhiḥ saṃprakīrtitāḥ // K_743 //	tad-mUla-tvAt tu te mOlAH RziBiH saMprakIrtitAH // K_743 //
   niṣpādyamānaṃ yair dṛṣṭaṃ tat kāryaṃ nṛguṇānvitaiḥ /	nizpAdyamAnam yEH dRzwam tat kAryam nR-guNa-anvitEH /
   vṛddhā vā yadi vāvṛddhās te vṛddhāḥ parikīrtitāḥ // K_744 //	vRdDAH vA yadi vA-avRdDAH te vRdDAH parikIrtitAH // K_744 //
   upaśravaṇasaṃbhoga- kāryākhyānopacihnitāḥ /	upaSravaNa-saMBoga kArya-AKyAna-upacihnitAH /

   sāmantāḥ sādhanaṃ pūrvam aniṣṭoktau guṇānvitāḥ /	sAmantAH sADanam pUrvam anizwa-uktO guNa-anvitAH /
   dviguṇās tūttarā jñeyā tato 'nye triguṇā matāḥ // K_746 //	dviguNAH tu-uttarA jQeyA tatas anye triguNAH matAH // K_746 //
   eko yadvan nayet sīmām ubhayor īpsitaḥ kvacit /	ekaH yadvat nayet sImAm uBayoH IpsitaH kvacid /
   mastake kṣitim āropya raktavāsāḥ samāhitāḥ // K_747 //	mastake kzitim Aropya rakta-vAsAH samAhitAH // K_747 //
   bhayavarjitabhūpena sarvābhāve svayaṃkṛtā // K_748 //	Baya-varjita-BUpena sarva-aBAve svayaMkRtAH // K_748 //
   kṣetrakūpataḍāgānāṃ kedārārāmayor api /	kzetra-kUpa-taxAgAnAm kedAra-ArAmayoH api /
   gṛhaprāsādāvasatha- nṛpadevagṛheṣu ca // K_749 //	gRha-prAsAda-AvasaTa nRpa-deva-gRhezu ca // K_749 //
   bahūnāṃ tu gṛhītānāṃ na sarve nirṇayaṃ yadi /	bahUnAm tu gRhItAnAm na sarve nirNayam yadi /
   kuryur bhayād vā lobhād vā dāpyās tūttamasāhasam // K_750 //	kuryuH BayAt vA loBAt vA dApyAH tu-uttamasAhasam // K_750 //
   sīmācaṅkramaṇe kośe pādasparśe tathaiva ca /	sImA-caFkramaNe koSe pAda-sparSe taTA-eva ca /
   tripakṣapakṣasaptāhaṃ daivarājikam iṣyate // K_751 //	tri-pakza-pakza-sapta-aham dEva-rAjikam izyate // K_751 //
   mekhalābhramaniṣkāsa- gavākṣān noparodhayet /	meKalA-Brama-nizkAsa gavAkzAt na-uparoDayet /
   praṇālīṃ gṛhavāstuṃ ca pīḍayan daṇḍabhāg bhavet // K_752 //	praNAlIm gRha-vAstum ca pIxayan daNxa-BAj Bavet // K_752 //
   niveśasamayād ūrdhvaṃ naite yojyāḥ kadācana /	niveSa-samayAt UrDvam na-ete yojyAH kadAcana /
   dṛṣṭipātaṃ praṇālīṃ ca na kuryāt paraveśmamu // K_753 //	dRzwi-pAtam praNAlIm ca na kuryAt para-veSmamu // K_753 //
   viṇmūtrodakavapraṃ ca vahniśvabhraniveśanam /	viz-mUtra-udaka-vapram ca vahni-SvaBra-niveSanam /
   aratnidvayam utsṛjya parakuḍyān niveśayet // K_754 //	aratni-dvayam utsRjya para-kuxyAt niveSayet // K_754 //
   sarve janāḥ sadā yena prayānti sa catuṣpathaḥ /	sarve janAH sadA yena prayAnti sa catuzpaTaH /
   aniruddho yathākālaṃ rājamārgaḥ sa ucyate // K_755 //	anirudDaH yaTAkAlam rAjamArgaH saH ucyate // K_755 //
   na tatra ropayet kiṃcin nopahanyāt tu kenacit /	na tatra ropayet kiMcid na-upahanyAt tu kenacid /
   guruācāryanṛpādīnāṃ mārgādānāt tu daṇḍabhāk // K_756 //	guru-AcArya-nRpa-AdInAm mArga-AdAnAt tu daNxa-BAj // K_756 //
   yas tatra saṃkaraśvabhrān vṛkṣāropaṇam eva ca /	yaH tatra saMkara-SvaBrAn vRkza-AropaNam eva ca /
   kāmāt purīṣaṃ kuryāc ca tasya daṇḍas tu māṣakaḥ // K_757 //	kAmAt purIzam kuryAt ca tasya daNxaH tu mAzakaH // K_757 //
   taṭākodyānatīrthāni yo 'medhyena vināśayet /	tawAka-udyAna-tIrTAni yaH ameDyena vinASayet /
   amedhyaṃ śodhayitvā tu daṇḍayet pūrvasāhasam // K_758 //	ameDyam SoDayitvA tu daNxayet pUrva-sAhasam // K_758 //
   dūṣayet siddhatīrthāni sthāpitāni mahātmabhiḥ /	dUzayet sidDa-tIrTAni sTApitAni mahAtmaBiH /
   puṇyāni pāvanīyāni prāpnuyāt pūrvasāhasam // K_759 //	puNyAni pAvanIyAni prApnuyAt pUrva-sAhasam // K_759 //
   sīmāmadhye tu jātānāṃ vṛkṣāṇāṃ kṣetrayor dvayoḥ /	sImA-maDye tu jAtAnAm vRkzANAm kzetrayoH dvayoH /
   phalaṃ puṣpaṃ ca sāmānyaṃ kṣetrasvāmiṣu nirdiśet // K_760 //	Palam puzpam ca sAmAnyam kzetra-svAmizu nirdiSet // K_760 //
   anyakṣetre tu jātānāṃ śākhā yatrānyasaṃśritāḥ /	anya-kzetre tu jAtAnAm SAKAH yatra-anya-saMSritAH /
   svāminaṃ taṃ vijānīyād yasya kṣetreṣu saṃśritāḥ // K_761 //	svAminam tam vijAnIyAt yasya kzetrezu saMSritAH // K_761 //
   asvāmyanumatenaiva saṃskāraṃ kurute tu yaḥ /	asvAmi-anumatena-eva saMskAram kurute tu yaH /
   gṛhodyānataṭākānāṃ saṃskartā labhate na tu // K_762 //	gRha-udyAna-tawAkAnAm saMskartA laBate na tu // K_762 //
   vyayaṃ svāmini cāyāte na nivedya nṛpe yadi /	vyayam svAmini ca-AyAte na nivedya nRpe yadi /
   athāvedya prayuktas tu tadgataṃ labhate vyayam // K_763 //	aTa-Avedya prayuktaH tu tad-gatam laBate vyayam // K_763 //
   aśaktito na dadyāc cet khilārtho yat kṛto vyayaḥ /	aSaktitaH na dadyAt ced Kila-arTaH yat kRtaH vyayaH /
